Chapter 2951: Reuniting the Shattered Sphere

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

After pondering the possibility of “exploiting the loophole in the Heavenly Dao,” Song Shuhang contacted Senior White and Senior White Two.

The concept of “two different beings proving the Dao and becoming immortal simultaneously” was a clue left by Heavenly Dao White after his near-transcendence.

Later, Senior White Two left this clue as “homework” for Song Shuhang, asking him to think about how “two different beings could prove the Dao simultaneously.”

Now that Song Shuhang had a lead, he remembered the “homework” and decided it was time to turn it in.

He opened the “Cultivator Chat System,” pulled up Senior White and Senior White Two from his friend list, and created a temporary discussion group.

The system notified him: *[Pet owner (text blurred, crossed out) close friend]White Two and [Admin]White have joined the temporary discussion group!*

“Done with the resurrection?” asked the present-world Senior White.

“What’s up?” inquired Senior White Two.

The new Heavenly Dao proving his Dao was such a significant event that even the dormant Senior White Two had been awakened. Normally, Senior White Two, who experienced intermittent bouts of drowsiness, would sleep for extended periods. But this time, his drowsiness had been forcibly dispelled. Because of his poor sleep, his mental state was a bit unstable.

Song Shuhang replied, “Present-world Senior White, I’m still in the process of resurrecting—just a little longer, and I’ll be done. No need to worry. As for Nine Serenities Senior White, I do have something to report.”

“What kind of ridiculous titles are those?” Senior White Two retorted, clearly displeased.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

Driven by a strong survival instinct, Song Shuhang had deliberately chosen to distinguish between the two Senior Whites by adding geographic descriptors, the most ordinary and non-confrontational way to differentiate them!

Currently, as his “Indestructible Whale Gold Core” hadn’t yet restored his resurrection cooldown, Song Shuhang’s survival instincts were terrifyingly strong. There was no way he would dare to call them “White Two” or “White Yoohoo!”

“Titles should indeed be distinct,” said Senior White after a brief thought. “You don’t need to add ‘present-world’ for me, but you can add ‘Nine Serenities’ when referring to Nine Serenities White.”

Senior White Two was speechless.

If it weren’t for his sleep deprivation and poor mental state, he would have immediately argued with the present-world White.

Senior White continued, “Does this sudden Dao-proving by the Confucian Daoist have anything to do with you, Shuhang?”

Song Shuhang nodded, “Yes, it should be related to the ritual held by the Northern Emperor, Daoist Red Scarf, and Cheng Goudan using the ‘Heavenly Court fragments’ within my Core World. However, I don’t know how they managed to elevate Daoist Senior to the position of the Immortal Heavenly Dao.”

After a brief pause, Senior White said, “So, the Confucian Daoist didn’t undergo a regular ‘Dao-proving,’ but instead took some kind of shortcut. White, has there been any activity on the Nine Serenities side?”

Under normal circumstances, once the Dao-proving process was completed, a corresponding “Nine Serenities Ruler” would emerge from the source of the Nine Serenities World!

The Heavenly Dao and the Nine Serenities Ruler share all memories before the Dao-proving. However, the Nine Serenities Ruler’s personality might change in the future due to the influence of the Nine Serenities’ source.

“There’s been some movement, which is why I’m a bit busy,” said Senior White Two.

Song Shuhang was puzzled, “I checked through Song Youyou, but I didn’t sense anything wrong in the Nine Serenities? There’s no movement in the source either.”

“That’s because you’re not me,” Senior White Two replied.

Song Shuhang was confused.

“The movement in the Nine Serenities is something only I can clearly sense. After all, I’ve been entangled with it for so long,” Senior White Two explained without further delay, “It’s Fat Ball... My instincts tell me that Fat Ball might be about to resurrect, reuniting the shattered sphere.”

Song Shuhang was startled. “Fat Ball is going to resurrect?”

He was still traumatized when it came to Fat Ball.

Upon hearing this news, the hair on his arms stood on end.

Moreover... why would Daoist Senior’s Dao-proving lead to Fat Ball’s resurrection?

Did the script get mixed up somewhere?

Shouldn’t there be a Daoist Two Ruler?

“Could Daoist Senior be Fat Ball’s backup plan?”

“No, Daoist Senior is the leader of the Confucian Thirteen Tribulation Immortals—there’s no way he’s Fat Ball’s backup plan.”

“It must be an issue with the Ancient Heavenly Court fragments.”

With his Immortal-level computational power, Song Shuhang quickly pulled out every clue related to the “thread” in his mind.

Ancient Heavenly Court fragments, the Dao of the Heavenly Dao, Fat Ball’s backup plan to complete itself, and the fact that Fairy Cheng Lin, the Northern Emperor, and others used the Heavenly Court fragments to push Daoist Senior into the position of Heavenly Dao. Moreover, the fact that the Nine Serenities didn’t produce a “Daoist Ruler,” but instead, the shattered Fat Ball is now reuniting.

One by one, the clues were pulled out, and Song Shuhang’s mind formed a clear conjecture.

His guess was probably very close to the truth.

“I’ll confirm this with Cheng Goudan later.”

As he thought about this, Song Shuhang replied to Senior White Two, “So, Senior White, are you trying to stop Fat Ball from resurrecting?”

“No,” Senior White Two replied seriously, “I’m looting Fat Ball’s inheritance.”

Song Shuhang was confused.

Senior White Two explained, “Since Fat Ball was thoroughly finished, I knew about its inheritance, but I wasn’t particularly interested in taking it. I thought I’d leave it for your Song Youyou to play a treasure hunt game with when you had the time.”

Song Shuhang was startled.

“But now that Fat Ball might reunite the shattered sphere at any moment, I need to raid its inheritance grounds before it recovers. I’ll leave it a note reminding it that I borrowed all the treasures, with an infinite-year repayment period,” Senior White Two added mischievously.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

At this point, he couldn’t help but touch his chest, which had already started to heal, feeling his heartbeat up close.

Listen, does the sound of his glass heart beating have a hint of heartbreak?

Overlord Song felt like he had lost another billion today.

Fat Ball’s inheritance left in the Nine Serenities, and several of them at that!

If he had raided them all, it might have been enough to pay off his massive debt to Senior White... But now, they all belonged to someone with the last name “White.”

“Oh, right, what did you want to say when you added us? I’m pretty busy right now, so make it quick,” Senior White Two urged.

He was currently sleep-deprived, mentally exhausted, and still had to force his fatigued body to raid Fat Ball’s inheritance and lair—such a tiring task.

“I came to turn in my homework, Senior White,” Song Shuhang replied.

“What homework?” Senior White Two asked, confused.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

Senior White Two, you assigned me this homework, and you actually forgot about it?

Chapter 2952: Why Push So Hard?

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

“This is about the possibility of two different entities achieving the Dao simultaneously,” Song Shuhang replied.

On the other end, Senior White Two remained silent for a while.

“Have you found the answer?” Senior White Two asked, his tone suddenly serious.

Song Shuhang nodded. “I’ve got a bit of a clue. Earlier, after the ‘Daoist Senior’ achieved Dao, he used the Heavenly Dao’s authority to calculate some of the information related to my ‘Path to Immortality.’ This information contains the concepts of ‘dead beyond dead, neither alive nor dead.’”

“What’s the principle behind this Path to Immortality?” Present-World Senior White asked.

“I haven’t figured it out yet,” Song Shuhang replied.

Senior White Two said, “Present-World White, don’t make it hard on Shuhang. The principles behind immortality are too complex. It’s impossible for him to comprehend them fully in such a short time. Besides, even if he doesn’t grasp the ‘principle,’ as long as this is confirmed as a ‘Path to Immortality,’ and has been verified by the Heavenly Dao, then even without understanding the principle, Shuhang can still achieve Dao if he keeps cultivating it.”

The principle isn’t important; what matters is that it’s a Path to Immortality. Just keep pushing forward.

Senior White agreed. “Makes sense.”

Song Shuhang was speechless.

Are the two Senior Whites teaming up to mess with me?

Senior White said, “Shuhang, go ahead and share your thoughts.”

“I’ve actually been trying to deduce the principle of this Path to Immortality... During the process, this ‘neither alive nor dead’ Path to Immortality inspired another idea in me!” Song Shuhang explained. “Back then, the clue left by the Heavenly Dao White was ‘two different entities achieving Dao simultaneously,’ but it didn’t mention whether these two entities were dead or alive.”

“So, you’re considering the possibility of one entity being alive and the other dead. The living one achieves Dao normally, while the dead one tags along in a ‘death state’ to become immortal?” Senior White Two followed Song Shuhang’s line of thinking.

Song Shuhang nodded. “Right. If one of the entities is dead, could this loophole in the Heavenly Dao be exploited?”

Neither of the Senior Whites responded immediately. They each began thinking and calculating.

After a while...

“There’s a problem... If it’s dead, how does it achieve immortality?” Senior White asked.

“The concept of immortality in the Heavenly Dao includes the idea of ‘undying and indestructible.’ If you attempt to use ‘death’ to achieve Dao, it might conflict with that concept,” Senior White Two said, rubbing his chin.

“There’s also another issue. How does the ‘alive’ side cooperate with the ‘dead’ side’s Path to Immortality to allow them to achieve Dao together?” Senior White added.

Song Shuhang thought for a long time before asking, “So, is the plan of one alive and one dead not feasible?”

“Not necessarily. Our understanding of ‘Heavenly Dao’ and ‘immortality’ is still limited. Your idea is at least a starting point. There’s a chance it can be further developed,” Senior White Two said.

Senior White chimed in, “Speaking of further development, I just had a thought—I’m quite interested in how the Confucian Daoist achieved ‘immortality.’ Maybe there’s a connection between the two?”

“What’s the theory behind the Confucian Daoist’s immortal achievement?” Senior White Two asked.

“I suspect the Daoist Senior’s achievement of Dao might be related to the ‘Ancient Heavenly Court Fragments’ and the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball’s ‘self-completion plan.’ We can ask a few of the involved parties for more details. Senior White, hold on a second; let me pull someone in,” Song Shuhang said.

After passing the ‘neither alive nor dead’ Path to Immortality data to Song Shuhang, the Daoist Heavenly Dao immediately went off to adjust to some of the ‘Heavenly Dao’s authority.’

Since the 8.5th Heavenly Dao is destined to be temporary, the Daoist Senior must race against time to fulfill everyone’s desires within the limited time available.

He’s working to undo the ‘incomplete resurrection’ side effects for his junior brothers.

He’s lifting the ancestral curse from the ‘Eight-Armed Primordial Demon.’

He’s breaking the shackles on the immortals from the ‘Ancient Heavenly Court’ for Fairy Cheng Lin.

And if time permits, he’d like to do a favor for little friend Tyrant Song, to settle an old debt.

The Daoist is quite busy.

So, Song Shuhang didn’t want to disturb the Daoist Senior.

He opened his ‘Cultivation Chat System’ friend list, lightly tapped Fairy Cheng Lin’s name, and added her to a temporary discussion group.

System Notification: [Blacklist 1: Deader than Dead Fairy] Fairy Goudan has joined the discussion group.

Fairy Cheng Lin: “???”

Song Shuhang: “(。・∀・)ノ゙ Hi, Fairy Goudan~”

Fairy Cheng Lin: “???”

Fairy Cheng Lin: “Why push so hard? Song Goudan, I don’t care why you pulled me in, but just for calling me that, goodbye—no, forever goodbye!”

“Fairy Cheng Lin, please wait. It’s not me who’s looking for you; Senior White wants to ask you something,” Song Shuhang hurriedly said.

Fairy Cheng Lin glanced at the two Whites in the discussion group. “...”

“Master White, what do you need?” Fairy Cheng Lin asked.

Senior White nodded and asked, “Fairy Cheng Lin, could you share the principle behind the Daoist Senior’s achievement of immortality?”

“The 8.5th Heavenly Dao Plan?” Fairy Cheng Lin asked back.

Senior White Two said, “So, it wasn’t the 9th Heavenly Dao... Interesting.”

“The plan has already succeeded, so sharing some details isn’t a problem,” Fairy Cheng Lin replied.

She then explained the details of the ‘8.5th Heavenly Dao Plan’ to the two Senior Whites.

After hearing the plan’s details, even Senior White Two couldn’t help but praise, “Fairy Cheng Lin, the plan you all devised is truly astonishing.”

The plan was bold yet meticulous.

Most importantly, it succeeded.

As long as it succeeds, no matter how risky or aggressive the plan was, it will be seen as perfect.

“Thank you for the compliment, Maswter White. Now that I’ve explained everything, can I leave the group?” Fairy Cheng Lin asked.

“Fairy Cheng Lin, please hold on. I’d like you to stay in the group. The next topic we’re discussing might require your input,” Senior White requested.

Initially ready to bid Song Goudan a permanent farewell, Fairy Cheng Lin pondered for a moment after Senior White’s request and then nodded. “Alright, I’ll give you this favor.”

“Thank you,” Senior White said with a slight smile before continuing, “Also, would the Daoist Heavenly Dao’s situation count as two different entities achieving immortality?”

The Fat Ball is an independent entity, and the 8.5th Heavenly Dao ‘Daoist’ is also an independent entity.

“That’s right! The 8.5th Heavenly Dao consists of the Daoist Senior plus the Heavenly Dao Ball, making them two distinct entities!” Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up.

“But this isn’t ‘simultaneous achievement.’ What we need are two different entities achieving Dao at the same time,” Senior White Two pointed out.

Senior White nodded. “Yes, but... this is still a direction to explore. By combining the ‘neither alive nor dead’ Path to Immortality that Shuhang mentioned earlier, we might be able to have two ‘neither alive nor dead’ entities complement each other’s flaws. Then, using the 8.5th Heavenly Dao’s method of self-completion, we could achieve the possibility of ‘simultaneous achievement.’”

Chapter 2953: The Second Eye

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

A missing Heavenly Dao Fat Ball + “Heavenly Dao Completion Plan” + a Daoist willing to sacrifice himself to complete the Heavenly Dao = two Heavenly Daos existing in the same era.

However, in this situation, while both the “Heavenly Dao Fat Ball” and the “Daoist” are considered the Heavenly Dao of the 8th era, they didn’t achieve enlightenment at the same time...

Moreover, the Daoist’s ability to attain the 8.5th era’s immortality hinges on the “Heavenly Dao Fat Ball” being gone.

If the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball were still alive before the ritual was completed, the Daoist’s sacrifice to complete the Heavenly Dao would only serve to perfect the “Heavenly Dao Fat Ball,” essentially sending a lamb to the slaughter and filling in the Fat Ball’s missing parts to make it a perfect sphere!

What Song Shuhang and Senior White want is for “two different entities to achieve immortality simultaneously,” so they can’t follow the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball and Daoist model.

However, there’s one thing to be borrowed from the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball and Daoist model—the concept that two incomplete entities can achieve enlightenment simultaneously as the Heavenly Dao of the same era!

As long as these two incomplete entities can complement each other—just like the Daoist completing the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball—there’s a chance, with the right manipulation, for them to achieve immortality together.

Senior White’s idea was to use Song Shuhang’s “neither life nor death” Eternal Life Path attribute to see if it could create two complementary entities—one that’s half-dead, the other half-alive?

Senior White described his idea in the temporary discussion group.

...

“So, what Senior White is suggesting is that before attaining ‘immortality,’ we should first damage the two candidates for enlightenment—damage them to the point of losing part of their existence, similar to the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball. The parts they lose should be able to complement each other, like one losing the upper half of their body while the other loses the lower half?” Senior White Two mused.

Senior White nodded, “That’s the idea.”

“But Shuhang’s ‘neither life nor death’ Eternal Life Path might not necessarily create two complementary incomplete entities,” Senior White Two pondered.

Finally, Song Shuhang found an opportunity to speak up: “In that case, we can ask @Cheng Lin Fairy... Cheng Lin Fairy, when the Daoist was completing the Heavenly Dao, was he fully intact? Or was he missing parts?”

“Missing parts,” Cheng Lin Fairy replied.

Song Shuhang pressed further, “What was missing?”

“The Confucian Sage left behind a book called ‘Confucian Classics,’ which had the ability to bite off part of the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball’s existence. The Daoist used the ‘Confucian Classics’ to activate this ability and bit off a part of himself,” Cheng Lin Fairy explained.

Song Shuhang: “...”

The Daoist was ruthless.

Being cruel to oneself is true cruelty.

“Is the Confucian Sage’s ‘Confucian Classics’ still usable?” Senior White Two asked.

Cheng Lin Fairy shook her head, “I’m afraid not. The Sage’s innate ability, which was attached to the ‘Confucian Classics,’ only manifested when the Daoist activated the book... It was an added effect from the Sage, not an inherent skill of the book itself.”

Senior White from the present world sighed in regret, “What a pity. If we could have studied the Confucian Sage’s ability, perhaps Nine Serenities White and I could have replicated it.”

“How about we wait until the Daoist is free, and I’ll retrieve the ‘Confucian Classics’ to see if there’s any trace of the Sage’s power left?” Song Shuhang suggested.

The “Confucian Classics” is officially in the care of Creation Fairy, but it was borrowed by Mad Blade Three Waves and eventually handed over to the Daoist.

As Song Shuhang spoke, a strange “resonance of the Great Dao” echoed through the void of the heavens and all realms.

This was the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, the “Daoist,” after his ascension, becoming familiar with the Heavenly Dao’s laws and beginning his first attempt to harness the power of the Great Dao.

In other words, it was the new Heavenly Dao’s first command to the heavens and all realms, a direct intervention by the Heavenly Dao.

Under the Daoist’s attempt, a “fate-altering” rule descended from the void.

The Confucian Golden Lotus World opened automatically.

The Second Tribulation Immortal, Wen Zi.

The Third Tribulation Immortal, Yan Zi.

The Seventh Tribulation Immortal, the dull Chi Zi.

The Eleventh Tribulation Immortal, Yu Zi.

Four Confucian Tribulation Immortals, plus Yuan Zi, possessed by a strand of the Kun King’s consciousness, stepped out of the Confucian Golden Lotus World simultaneously.

That “fate-altering” power fell upon them.

The “death karma” that lingered over Wen Zi, Yan Zi, Chi Zi, and Yu Zi was directly severed.

The faint aura of death on them vanished, replaced by boundless vitality.

Their previously “incomplete resurrection” was fully completed under the power of the 8.5th Heavenly Dao.

Each of the thirteen Confucian Tribulation Immortals had the potential to attain immortality... Now, with these four Tribulation Immortals fully resurrected, their bodies complete, all they needed was time to eventually take the final step towards becoming Eternal Beings.

The “Yuan Zi” nearby was also enveloped by the fate-altering power.

However, the Heavenly Dao’s power only flashed across his body before disappearing, as if something had changed, yet nothing seemed different.

The Second Tribulation Immortal, Wen Zi, glanced at “Yuan Zi” in confusion... Could it be that Yuan Zi’s consciousness hadn’t fully dissipated? His body wasn’t just an empty shell, but rather waiting for the right moment to regain consciousness?

Aside from the five Confucian Tribulation Immortals who remained, the Daoist’s power spread across the heavens and all realms, scattering six more strands of “fate-altering” power.

Among these six, two had the attribute of “completing an incomplete resurrection array.” The remains and resurrection arrays of these two Tribulation Immortals had always been secretly kept by the Daoist.

The other four had the effect of healing severe injuries—over the years, four heavily wounded Confucian Tribulation Immortals had secretly taken turns guarding the Confucian sect.

However, due to their severe injuries, they spent most of their time in seclusion, healing.

Now, under the Daoist’s power, the injuries of these four Tribulation Immortals were healed.

“Senior Brother.” When the four Tribulation Immortals opened their eyes, they couldn’t help but tear up.

What their master couldn’t accomplish, their senior brother had done!

After taking care of his thirteen junior brothers’ aftereffects in one go, the Daoist slightly frowned—yet there was no trace of his youngest junior brother, the Glazed Scholar.

The Daoist sighed deeply.

He gently closed the “Confucian Classics,” and suddenly, an object emerged from within, lightly landing in his hand.

It was an eye, seemingly ordinary at first glance.

Yet, this eye was one that could make cultivators across the heavens and Nine Serenities tremble—it was feared by all because of Tyrannical Song’s reputation.

“The teacher’s eye.” The Daoist carefully cradled it.

The appearance of the Confucian Sage’s eye was a gesture of comfort for the Daoist, telling him that he had done well.

The Daoist stared blankly at the eye in his hand.

After pondering for a moment, the Daoist suddenly tossed it lightly.

The “Confucian Classics” and the “Sage’s Eye” both vanished into the void, heading in Song Shuhang’s direction.

Chapter 2954: A Scene Only Visible with Two Eyes

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

The Ritual Code was something the Little Junior Sister unearthed, so it was returned to her for safekeeping.

The second Sage’s Eye was given to Tyrannical Song as a token of gratitude from Daozi on behalf of the Confucianists.

Tyrannical Song had done too much for the Confucians.

Even this 8.5th Heavenly Dao Ceremony was conducted using Tyrannical Song’s core world and fragments of the Heavenly Court—although the Northern Daoist had already negotiated the borrowing terms with Tyrannical Song, the very act of lending itself was a favor.

As the saying goes, “A drop of water shall be returned with a spring.”

Since Tyrannical Song already had one Sage’s Eye, the second eye should also be handed to him.

The teacher would probably agree with this decision.

After all, in all the worlds, only Tyrannical Song could wield the teacher’s eye so well, making the Sage’s Eye famous.

The Sage’s Eye and Tyrannical Song were fated to be together!

—

At the same time, in the core world...

Tyrannical Song’s upper body had already regenerated. He reached out, summoning a garment, and draped it over himself. He also preemptively wrapped a sheet around his body.

Once properly dressed, he summoned all his accessories back to him.

Particularly the Song Fat Ball Windbreaker!

With the Nine Nether Fat Ball Elder about to resurrect, the presence of the Song Fat Ball had become increasingly dangerous—no one could guarantee when it might suddenly connect with the resurrected Fat Ball Elder and regain its memories.

To prevent any accidents, Tyrannical Song recalled the Song Fat Ball Windbreaker and maintained the connection between the core world and the Evil Lotus World. It would be best to send the Song Fat Ball Windbreaker to Senior White Two.

After all, only Senior White Two could securely suppress the Song Fat Ball Windbreaker at this point.

As Tyrannical Song was recalling his accessories, a thick book suddenly broke through the air.

The book hurtled toward him with the sound of wind and thunder, exuding an imposing aura.

“Who dares attack my princess!” Virtuous Snake Beauty darted out, her electronic voice clear and powerful. She wrapped her body protectively around Tyrannical Song, shielding him from the book.

Clang!

The book struck the forehead of Virtuous Snake Beauty, producing a metallic clang.

“It’s the Ritual Code. It seems that Senior Daozi sensed we needed it, so he sent it back. The Heavenly Dao is terrifying; there’s practically no privacy in front of it. Thankfully, Senior Daozi is a gentleman. If it were someone with more sinister inclinations, who knows how much blackmail material they’d gather and store?” Tyrannical Song mused as he bent down to pick up the Ritual Code.

Virtuous Snake Beauty rubbed her forehead.

Then, she looked at Tyrannical Song.

After picking up the Ritual Code, Tyrannical Song casually flipped through it.

Virtuous Snake Beauty was speechless.

I got hit!

My forehead got smashed by the Ritual Code with a loud clang!

Seeing that Tyrannical Song’s attention was entirely focused on the Ritual Code, Virtuous Snake Beauty rolled her eyes and collapsed to the ground, playing dead like a limp snake. “Ah, the wind is blowing.”

After her long-forgotten play-dead routine, Virtuous Snake Beauty lay on the ground, slyly peeking at Tyrannical Song.

And then... she saw a scene that made her scales stand on end!

Tyrannical Song had pulled an eye out from the Ritual Code.

This eye looked very ordinary, indistinguishable from a normal human eye.

However, any practitioner this year who saw this eye would immediately recognize it!

The second Confucian Sage’s Eye!

Virtuous Snake Beauty felt as if she heard a game-like notification sound in her mind: “Ding~ Congratulations, player ‘Tyrannical Song’ has collected the complete green set ‘Confucian Sage’s Eyes’ (Left) (Right).”

“A Sage’s Eye?” Tyrannical Song lifted the eye gently with his mind power.

At the same time, a blood web emerged from the void.

This was a blood web formed by a drop of Confucian Sage’s Blood that had assimilated with Tyrannical Song’s body. The blood web contained some of Tyrannical Song’s precious organs that couldn’t be regenerated with normal resurrection methods.

For example, the Third Divine Eye and the other Confucian Sage’s Eye...

“A pair of Sage’s Eyes.” Tyrannical Song held them with his mind power.

He actually gathered both of them?

So... should he try putting them on? The thought suddenly crossed Tyrannical Song’s mind.

The moment that thought surfaced, Creation Fairy sensed it and appeared.

She gently approached Tyrannical Song from behind, extending her hands to cover his eye sockets.

Painless eye removal!

Creation Fairy deftly plucked out Tyrannical Song’s recently regenerated eyes and kept them safe for future use.

Then, she skillfully inserted the pair of Confucian Sage’s Eyes into Tyrannical Song’s eye sockets.

The Third Divine Eye also lazily returned to its place in the void.

The Sage’s Blood enveloped the other precious organs, guiding them back into position.

Virtuous Snake Beauty lay on the ground, her head tilted as she stopped pretending to be dead. She watched Tyrannical Song with curiosity—she wanted to see what special changes Tyrannical Song would undergo after acquiring a complete set of eyes.

Hot!

Scorching heat!

As the pair of Sage’s Eyes were placed, Tyrannical Song felt his eye sockets heat up crazily.

Even with his high pain tolerance, the burning sensation was intense—an indication that the temperature was extraordinary.

Luckily, Tyrannical Song’s strength had already reached the Slaying Three Corpses Tribulation Immortal level; otherwise, his eye sockets would have been seared like before by the Confucian Sage’s Eyes.

Due to the constant rise in temperature from the Sage’s Eyes, Tyrannical Song’s eye sockets began secreting Tribulation Immortal Tears, which were then evaporated by the Sage’s Eyes, forming a white mist that enveloped the area in front of his eyes.

After a while...

Tyrannical Song finally adjusted to the Confucian Sage’s Eyes.

He slowly opened his eyes.

The Sage’s Eyes moved nimbly within their sockets.

“Is it foggy?” Tyrannical Song asked.

Pavilion Master Chu poetically replied, “Those aren’t fog; they’re your tears.”

“How about we collect them?” Tyrannical Song suggested—Tribulation Immortal Tears turned into mist were valuable materials for artifact crafting.

As they spoke, Tyrannical Song’s eyes began to shift slightly.

The focus of the Sage’s Eyes locked onto the cloud of ‘mist.’

The mist acted like a screen, and through this ‘screen,’ the Sage’s Eyes saw several fleeting images.

There was a fleeting image of Yun Quezi’s silhouette.

There was a scene of someone holding a child, looking lost.

There was an image of a person meticulously sewing a Confucian robe for a disciple.

There was a powerful arm gently writing Confucian characters on white paper.

Finally... the image froze on the Confucian characters.

Tyrannical Song couldn’t recognize the Confucian characters at all, but through the Confucian Sage’s Eyes, he could miraculously understand their meaning. The Sage’s Eyes had an auto-translate feature.

The Confucian characters contained the Sage’s analysis of his own innate ability.

And... its inheritance.

The Confucian Sage had researched and refined a method to turn his innate ability into a spell, to be passed down.

His research was successful, but also a failure.

—It was successful because the ability could indeed be passed down, but it was a failure because the cost was too great to be acceptable.

By consuming a Confucian Sage’s Eye and a Path of Longevity, one could gain the chance to inherit the Sage’s talent.

The success rate wasn’t even 100%...

Moreover, the Sage’s Eyes were different from Tyrannical Song’s eyes.

There were only two of them—no bulk supply!

The Sage wasn’t like Tyrannical Song, who had a habit of plucking out his own eyes.

In other words, at best, these two Sage’s Eyes could only allow two people to inherit the Sage’s talent, and that’s assuming things went perfectly.

Chapter 2955: Fellow Daoist Song’s Redemption

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

If luck isn’t on your side, not only could you fail to inherit the Confucian Sage’s “special talent,” but you might also lose the Sage’s eye... and an entire path to immortality!

The price is nothing short of devastating.

It’s a “do or die” situation!

Such a steep cost would stop even the most powerful beings across the myriad worlds in their tracks.

Even those who stand at the pinnacle of countless worlds and have achieved immortality typically just walk their own path to eternity.

Take the “Heavenly Emperor,” for instance. She possessed a “Heavenly Court Path” and a “Time Path” simultaneously—a rarity even in the vastness of all worlds!

But even the Heavenly Emperor didn’t hold both eternal methods at the same time. She passed the “Heavenly Court Path” to Jin Gua before stabilizing her immortality through the “Time Path.”

Without the Heavenly Emperor’s extraordinary methods, attempting to inherit the Confucian Sage’s “special talent” would mean falling from the immortal realm, even if you succeeded, down to the level of a tribulation immortal...

“The cost and the reward aren’t proportional at all,” Song Shuhang commented.

People might gamble with their lives, but no one would enter into a losing deal.

Exchanging a priceless “Confucian Sage’s eye” plus an entire path to immortality for a talent that might not even succeed? In a normal situation, that’s a deal you’d have to be crazy to take!

The Confucian Sage’s eye—how could that not be valuable?

Just one “Confucian Sage’s eye” had made cultivators across the myriad worlds tremble in fear!

And don’t even mention the path to immortality.

Since ancient times, there might not be enough immortals to average even one per world in the myriad worlds.

Who would be willing to burn through an entire path to immortality?

Except for someone like the Heavenly Emperor, who has unique circumstances, who else could afford such a thing?

“What happens with two Confucian Sage’s eyes?” Pavilion Master Chu couldn’t help but ask, curious.

Fengyi Qinmaster added, “So, the eye we just saw was the Confucian Sage’s?”

“Yes.” Song Shuhang nodded, then he described what he saw through the “pair of Confucian Sage’s eyes” and the Sage’s analysis of the “talent.”

Just as Song Shuhang finished his explanation, White Senior Two’s voice rang out, “We need this talent from the Confucian Sage.”

Core World and Evil Lotus World were closely connected at this moment, so even without using a “temporary group,” White Senior Two was keeping tabs on Song Shuhang.

“Indeed, if we could have two people inherit the Confucian Sage’s ‘devouring others’ existence’ talent... then we must obtain this ability,” Senior White agreed.

After all, there’s no other ability more suited to creating two “imperfect yet complementary” special beings than the Confucian Sage’s “devour the existence of others” technique.

If two people with the Confucian Sage’s talent devoured a part of each other before achieving enlightenment, they could theoretically achieve a “complementary enlightenment.”

“But won’t the cost be too great?” Song Shuhang asked.

“If it can result in two distinct beings achieving enlightenment simultaneously, the price is worth it,” White Senior Two responded.

Sometimes, an exchange that seems unbalanced becomes worthwhile under the right conditions.

“Also, the Confucian Sage’s plan is just a draft... we could refine it and reduce the cost,” Senior White added.

The Confucian Sage had only just begun exploring his talent, and he didn’t push it to its limits.

The hardest part is starting. With the Sage’s “starting point,” Senior White Two and Senior White could continue researching and make improvements.

“For example... we might be able to preserve the ‘Confucian Sage’s eyes’ after they’re used up,” White Senior Two said.

“How would we do that?” Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up.

“Don’t forget about your Immortal Whale Golden Core. It’s an incredible object, so don’t just treat it like a ‘rechargeable resurrection device.’” White Senior Two pointed out, “If you can bind the Confucian Sage’s eyes to your Immortal Whale Golden Core, then even if the Sage’s eyes are sacrificed or turned to ashes, the power of the Immortal Whale Golden Core could restore them from nothing.”

The Immortal Whale Golden Core is like an “immortal bone” with a cooldown. If you time it right, the Confucian Sage’s eyes, originally consumable, could become reusable, like a portable power bank.

“So, how do we bind them?” Song Shuhang’s eyes sparkled.

“That’s what we need to research. When the time comes, bring the Sage’s eyes and the Whale Golden Core to me, and I’ll study them thoroughly,” White Senior Two said.

“Similarly, it might be possible to recover some of the cost of using a path to immortality,” Senior White added.

Following the conversation, Song Shuhang tried to keep up with the advanced topic the two Seniors were discussing. He ventured, “Turn the ‘path to immortality’ into a kind of rechargeable battery, so after it’s used up, it can be recharged and reused. Or, make the cost a ‘partial use of the path to immortality,’ then restore it afterward?”

“That’s unlikely... the consumption of a path to immortality is a foundational part of the Confucian Sage’s plan,” Senior White shook his head.

“But before consuming your path to immortality, you could try backing it up—saving the understanding, data, and information related to the path. Then, if you can’t re-cultivate that path, you could at least pass it on to someone else,” White Senior Two chimed in, complementing Senior White’s thought.

It’s still uncertain whether a path to immortality consumed during the inheritance process could be cultivated again. If not, passing it on to someone close could at least minimize the loss.

One path to immortality per immortal.

If you step down from that path, someone else could step up to inherit it.

Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up. “Like that unwalked path to immortality stored in the merit network? Brilliant.”

He had two potential paths to immortality.

One was the “Non-Life, Non-Death” path.

The other was connected to the “Cultivation Chat” system.

The “Non-Life, Non-Death” path could be sacrificed.

However, the path connected to the “Cultivation Chat” system was too grand—it could only be completed from a perspective that surpasses immortality.

Song Shuhang didn’t have the confidence to master that path to immortality.

...

...

Meanwhile, the 8.5th Heavenly Dao’s “Daozi,” after resolving the lingering issues of the Confucian disciples, took a brief rest.

Then, he began to address “Song Woodenhead’s” obsession, bringing them salvation.

“To those fellow Daoists bound to the ancient Heavenly Court, as promised, I will grant you freedom on behalf of Song Daoist,” Daozi said, drawing a circle of light in the air.

Behind him, several “substitute avatars” emerged and stepped into the circle of light.

Chapter 2956: I’m Coming Out!

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

As each tribulation substitute appeared, they bowed respectfully in the direction of the Daozi.

These substitutes were created by binding the marks of immortals trapped in the “Heavenly Emperor’s Path of the Heavenly Court” and combining them with Song Woodenhead’s ghost hand techniques.

Now, Daozi was fulfilling his agreement with Song Woodenhead. These tribulation substitutes, representing their true selves, were expressing their gratitude to Daozi.

While bowing, the substitutes shifted their gaze behind Daozi, where a more mature version of Song Shuhang floated calmly, seated cross-legged in a meditative posture.

The tribulation substitutes nodded respectfully to the mature version of Song Shuhang before leaping into the glowing circle one by one.

In Song Shuhang’s Core World...

The Northern Emperor’s form trembled slightly, as if he had just lost something.

He was one of the few members of the Heavenly Court who had managed to escape death through his own backup plans. After his resurrection, the Northern Emperor was no longer bound by the “Path of the Heavenly Court.”

However, there remained a mark of him within the ancient Path of the Heavenly Court—this was why, when Song Woodenhead had appeared to rescue Pavilion Master Chu, there had been a “Northern Emperor” present in his golden spatial world. The “Northern Emperor” in Woodenhead’s space was a tribulation substitute formed from the mark left by the Northern Emperor.

This was also the reason why Puppet Fairy had refused to acknowledge the revived Northern Emperor as the original. She couldn’t sense the familiar aura she once recognized. In her puppet state, her way of identifying things was different from that of living beings.

But now, as the tribulation substitute jumped into the glowing circle and disappeared entirely, the Northern Emperor lost a trace of his icy aura, gaining a faint warmth instead.

His realm seemed to have been subtly liberated, increasing ever so slightly.

Apart from the Northern Emperor, several other ancient Heavenly Court immortals also experienced a change in their aura, achieving true freedom.

Back in the Core World...

Golden Cheng Lin covered her forehead with her hands, shielding her eyes.

At this moment, she didn’t want her companions to see her tearful, elated expression.

Memories of the days spent with her fellow Daoists, playing and fooling around in the ancient Heavenly Court, flooded her mind.

Now, all those companions were finally free from the restraints of the “Path of the Ancient Heavenly Court.” In the near future, they would all return from their sealed states.

“If you want to cry, just cry out loud,” Daoist Chixiao said with a smile. “After all, it’s Cheng Lin’s reputation on the line.”

Golden Cheng Lin was speechless.

Daoist Chixiao made a very good point, but now that he mentioned it, even though she really wanted to cry, Golden Cheng Lin found herself unable to shed a single tear.

She removed her hands from her eyes and laughed. “Daoist, the 8.5th Heavenly Dao Ceremony is complete... Next, according to the contract, I need to take Jin Gua’s ‘Mysterious Island Heavenly Court Fragment’ back to his island and hand over the ‘Emperor Seal.’ I’ll be back soon... In the meantime, I’ll leave the management of things in your capable hands.”

The Emperor Seal was merely a symbol of the Heavenly Emperor during the Ancient Heavenly Court and didn’t have any real power.

However, as per the contract, after Golden Cheng Lin handed over the Emperor Seal to Jin Gua, once everything was settled, the 8.5th Heavenly Dao “Daozi” would bestow the complete “Path of the Heavenly Emperor” upon Jin Gua, making him the one and only officially recognized second-generation Heavenly Emperor.

“Leave it to me,” Daoist Chixiao nodded.

“Well then, everyone, I’ll be back soon.” Golden Cheng Lin extended her hand, and the fragments of the Heavenly Court belonging to the “Mysterious Island” within Song Shuhang’s Core World floated up.

Additionally, a portion of the Heavenly Court fragments originally collected by the “Heavenly Dao Must Step Down Alliance” was also included as part of the payment to Jin Gua—the remaining Heavenly Court fragments would serve as Song Shuhang’s compensation.

This time, under Song Shuhang’s careful restraint, the Heavenly Court fragments from the “Mysterious Island” did not have their embedded “Path of the Heavenly Court” absorbed by the Core World.

After all, this was something Song Shuhang had promised Jin Gua, the Island Master!

However... the “Path of the Heavenly Court” within the Heavenly Court fragments collected by the “Heavenly Dao Must Step Down Alliance” was mostly licked clean by the Core World after the ceremony.

Golden Cheng Lin, carrying numerous Heavenly Court fragments, vanished into the void.

This journey to the Mysterious Island was not just to return the Heavenly Court fragments, but also to visit the Dragon Tomb on the island and see the “Golden Dragon Ancestor’s” resting place.

Now that Golden Cheng Lin’s obsession had been resolved, the 8.5th Heavenly Dao plan had succeeded, and the restraints on the ancient Heavenly Court immortals had been broken, everything was on track.

So, while there was still some time, she intended to visit the Dragon Tomb and meet the Golden Dragon Ancestor... and remind her that staying cooped up in the tomb for too long wasn’t good for her health.

...

Back in the Core World...

“Did Senior Daozi issue a second directive? What’s the instruction this time?” Song Shuhang asked.

The first directive was to relieve the Confucian school of the aftereffects of their incomplete resurrection, but what about this one?

In the temporary discussion group...

Fairy Cheng Lin replied, “It’s to release the restraints on the ancient Heavenly Court members.”

“Are all the ancient Heavenly Court members’ restraints being lifted? Wouldn’t Senior Jin Gua end up as the bachelor emperor?” Song Shuhang asked.

Wouldn’t this be a heavy burden for Senior Jin Gua, who had only just taken on the position of Heavenly Emperor?

“No worries. The ‘Path of the Heavenly Court’ for the second-generation Heavenly Emperor Jin Gua is different from the original... There’s no hidden danger, and it won’t be swallowed up as part of the ‘Heavenly Dao Completion Plan.’ So, in the future, he can gradually reintegrate the Heavenly Court members,” Fairy Cheng Lin explained.

A Heavenly Court with no hidden dangers, combined with the grand momentum of the “Heavenly Court Reestablishment” right before Daozi ascended to the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, had essentially served as an advertisement for Jin Gua.

In the future, there would be a wave of “returning to the Heavenly Court” from survivors scattered across the myriad worlds.

The second-generation Heavenly Emperor Jin Gua would be the ultimate beneficiary.

“Island Master Jin Gua is the second-generation Heavenly Emperor?” Song Shuhang asked, suddenly confused.

He remembered that Senior Copper Trigram had mentioned seeing two Heavenly Emperor tombs—one old and one new—on the Mysterious Island.

Even though they were just cenotaphs.

So why was Island Master Jin Gua still considered the second-generation Heavenly Emperor?

“Was Heavenly Emperor Dadazi the first generation?” Song Shuhang asked.

[Ding~ Your ‘good-for-nothing friend’ the Heavenly Emperor has remotely sent you one drop of energy, with a note: Senior Song, you called for me~]

See! This is the terrifying power of a top-tier big shot.

As long as you say her name, she’ll sense it after running a series of data screening formulas.

Hold on.

[You revived?] Song Shuhang asked.

[Ah, after waiting so long... it’s time to revive. Senior Song, lift up your shirt~] the Heavenly Emperor transmitted her voice.

Song Shuhang: “???”

[I’m coming out,] the Heavenly Emperor replied.

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

Chapter 2957: Trouble? Bring Me Along!

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

“So it’s you, Sun Wukong Son of Heaven!”

“Then that makes me Song Iron Fan Shuhang, right?”

“Should I say something to coordinate with you?” Song Shuhang asked.

Celestial Thearch was speechless.

On this day, the Celestial Thearch realized that there are limits to human understanding. Even someone like her could be stumped by some of Song Shuhang’s lines, unable to grasp the underlying meaning and continue the conversation.

“How am I supposed to respond to that?” the Celestial Thearch asked.

Song Shuhang thought for a moment, then said, “Maybe it’s better if you don’t respond... If you force it, it’s going to get really awkward for me.”

“I’ll look into what that means later,” the Celestial Thearch said. “I’ve got plenty of free time now that I’ve been resurrected.”

“Alright,” Song Shuhang replied.

Then he began to lift his shirt in cooperation.

But halfway through, he suddenly remembered something: “Celestial Thearch, why are you resurrecting inside my body?”

As expected, there must have been a reason she insisted that he annihilate her completely. Had she planted a spore in him the moment she died by his hand?

“Wanna guess?” the Celestial Thearch retorted.

Song Shuhang, dead serious, said, “Over the past year, I’ve grown to hate it when people ask me to guess things I have no clue about, so I can’t figure them out; and second, I hate it when people try to read my face for answers when I ask them ‘Wanna guess?’”

The Celestial Thearch laughed, “I’m the opposite... I love seeing the look of utter confusion on someone’s face when I ask them to guess.”

Song Shuhang was speechless.

As they were talking, a “lotus projection” formed on his body.

“It’s this thing?” Song Shuhang was startled.

He remembered this lotus projection. It was from when his Core World had recklessly tried to swallow the Celestial Thearch and lick her “Heavenly Court Dao,” resulting in this massive lotus projection. But it backfired. The Celestial Thearch had severed the giant lotus projection... And in the end, the projection became compensation for Song Shuhang’s Core World secretly licking the Celestial Thearch’s “Heavenly Court Fragment Dao.”

If not for the Celestial Thearch pulling it out now, Shuhang might have completely forgotten about it.

“So, you’ve been hiding in this lotus projection all along? Hiding in my body?”

“No, I’ve been hiding on Little Blackie the whole time~” the Celestial Thearch’s voice replied.

Black Soft Feather: “!!!”

You were hiding on me all this time? When did that happen? How did I not notice at all? Also... I’m not ‘Little Blackie!’

“Butter Song Baihua Huang... Guai Li Six Bean Phoenix.” Little Blackie pondered for a while, unsure what to say, so she just announced her full name.

“If I had hidden directly in you, with your connection to the lotus projection, you would have sensed it right away. But hiding on Little Blackie was easy. With my relationship with her, plus the ‘enlightenment’ and aura concealment I left with you before I died, it was almost impossible for you to notice me~” the Celestial Thearch continued.

Little Blackie: “...”

I just said my name, and you’re ignoring it. That’s rude.

Next to them, Song Shuhang thought for a moment, then mimicked the tone of the Virtuous Lamia, speaking seriously, “Lies obscure the truth and lead the outcome astray!”

Even if the lotus projection was on Black Soft Feather, there was no way he wouldn’t have sensed it. So... the Celestial Thearch wasn’t telling the truth. Or maybe she was mixing in some half-truths. Most likely, he got hit by something when he slashed her to death, or maybe when he floated to the ‘Celestial Thearch’s Throne Two’ during his resurrection.

“Heaven is jealous of geniuses, and they die young,” the Celestial Thearch replied.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

I can’t mess with her, I really can’t.

As they spoke, the lotus projection bloomed.

The lotus bud unfurled, and a tall figure stepped out from within.

The resurrected “Celestial Thearch” still retained Feather Rouzi’s basic appearance—perfectly proportioned long legs, silky smooth long hair. However, her expression seemed more mature compared to Feather Rouzi’s.

“This resurrection state is just right,” the resurrected Celestial Thearch said with a satisfied stretch.

The stretching motion highlighted Feather Rouzi’s stunning figure in every detail!

Creation Fairy raised her hands to cover Song Shuhang’s eyes, blocking his view. After all, these were her master’s eyes. Who knew what powerful functions they might have? What if Song Shuhang got excited and activated one of those powerful functions?

But Song Shuhang didn’t mind.

In fact, at his level of power, seeing things wasn’t limited to using the “eyes” as an organ. Besides, apart from the pair of Confucian Saint’s Eyes, he also had a third godly eye.

After the Celestial Thearch’s resurrection was complete, Song Shuhang reached up and gently poked the Fengyi Qin Lord’s claw on his head.

The Fengyi Qin Lord’s claw responded, “What? You almost poked my eye.”

There was a single eye on her claw.

“Look, it’s a fresh Celestial Thearch, alive and kicking,” Song Shuhang said.

The Fengyi Qin Lord’s claw fell silent.

“I told your main body before, I’m really familiar with the Celestial Thearch, so your main body shouldn’t be messing with the whole ‘resurrecting the Celestial Thearch’ thing. But she wouldn’t believe me,” Song Shuhang said.

The Fengyi Qin Lord’s claw fell silent again.

“But I was once killed by Senior Song~” the Celestial Thearch stepped on air, bent down, and with a tug, pulled the massive “lotus projection” off of Song Shuhang, casually tossing it into her spatial storage.

Even if it was used up, it was still hers, so she had to keep it.

“Should I congratulate you on your perfect resurrection?” Song Shuhang asked, as he checked the Celestial Thearch’s status in his “Cultivation Chat System” again.

Her status had already switched from “dead as can be” to “perfectly reborn.”

Perfect meant she had completely broken free from the “Heavenly Court Dao.”

“If you congratulate me, I still won’t have a red envelope to give you,” the Celestial Thearch replied.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

So shallow, do I look like I care about a red envelope?

“Now that I’m resurrected, I’ve got a bit of business to take care of,” the Celestial Thearch said.

“Causing trouble? Count me in!” Song Shuhang asked—not because he really wanted to join, but to find out what the Celestial Thearch was planning, to get some intel.

“Sure,” the Celestial Thearch smiled. “I’m going to chop down Cheng Lin, wanna come?”

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

“Right now, isn’t Senior Song Cheng Lin?” Black Soft Feather asked. “So you’re gonna chop down Senior Song?”

“Ah, I almost forgot about that,” the Celestial Thearch chuckled.

Then she formed her fingers into a sword and pointed it at Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang: “You’re serious?”

“Of course~ Time Dao: Sword of Years—Clouds Parting, Rivers Flowing,” the Celestial Thearch said as she thrust her finger sword at Song Shuhang.

Chapter 2958: A Signal Beyond the Heavens

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

At that moment, the Celestial Thearch and Song Shuhang were only about a meter apart—a distance so insignificant to those of their caliber that it was practically nonexistent.

Moreover, the Celestial Thearch had been resurrected in perfect form. At such a close range, if she were to make a move, thrusting her sword, no one across the myriad realms could evade it!

Just as the Celestial Thearch prepared to strike...

The Phoenix Master hastily explained, “It’s coming—this is the Celestial Thearch’s ultimate move—’Senile Dementia Sword!’ Anyone struck by this blade is doomed to wither into senility over the endless passage of time!”

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

See, this is why names are so important.

The same move, the same power, the same effect, but change the name, and the gravitas changes by an entire plane of existence.

‘Senile Dementia Sword’ compared to the Celestial Thearch’s announced ‘Sword of Time—Fleeting Clouds, Flowing Water for Ten Years’—both have the same nature, but the difference in prestige is staggering.

If my “Basic Fist Techniques, Part II” were renamed to “Meteor Fist—Shattering the Moon and Splitting the Mountain Peaks, Meteor Sweeping the Dawn Sky,” its prestige would probably shoot through the roof as well!

Even when facing the Celestial Thearch’s sword, Song Shuhang’s mind, enhanced by his “Slaying Three Corpses Tribulation Immortal” level, was still able to flash through these unrelated thoughts.

Of course, he hadn’t given up on resisting. His body instinctively tried to dodge as the Celestial Thearch struck.

But the one-meter range was too small, fully within the domain of the Celestial Thearch’s “Time Dao.”

The Celestial Thearch’s finger finally touched Song Shuhang!

Time and the force of years were violently propelled.

Under the influence of this strike, Song Shuhang’s body stiffened, unable to move.

In his pupils, countless streams of information rapidly processed—that was the Confucian Sage’s Eye, receiving information and converting it, feeding it back to Song Shuhang.

A few breaths later.

“Hahh~” The Celestial Thearch exhaled softly, withdrawing her finger.

“What did you do to Shuhang?” Pavilion Master Chu’s hair strand asked.

Pavilion Master Chu didn’t seem intent on attacking the Celestial Thearch. Given her level, she could naturally tell that the Celestial Thearch’s strike hadn’t harmed Song Shuhang.

“First, I poked Senior Song, who’s currently in Cheng Lin’s form, to collect some interest~ And, of course, to practice my technique for when I slice through the real Cheng Lin later. I’ll be more proficient by then.” The Celestial Thearch replied.

Pavilion Master Chu’s hair strand: “...”

“And also, I used that strike to end Senior Song’s long-standing ‘enlightenment’ state and give him part of the answer.” The Celestial Thearch continued.

Since Song Shuhang had cut her down once before, he’d been affected by the Celestial Thearch’s earlier primordial spirit’s “obliteration,” leaving him in a prolonged state of “enlightenment plus Dao comprehension.”

However, the problem with “enlightenment” is that if it lasts too long, it can lose its soul, the critical “flash of insight” during the moment of realization.

Thus, the Celestial Thearch took this opportunity to provide Song Shuhang with part of the correct answer, allowing him to exit the soulless state of enlightenment.

“What information did you give to Shuhang?” the Scarlet Heaven Sword asked.

It could feel the “Path of Longevity” aura on Song Shuhang becoming more complete. Was the Celestial Thearch giving Song Shuhang information that would complete his “Path of Longevity”?

“The ancient Heavenly Court, aside from a few constraints, has some similarities with Senior Song’s ‘Repair Chat System.’ The information I gave him was the complete details of that portion, along with my personal insights.” The Celestial Thearch replied.

The Stele Spirit spoke up, “Are you sure you have no ulterior motives towards Shuhang?”

“If I say I have no ulterior motives towards Senior Song, would you believe me?” the Celestial Thearch responded.

The Phoenix Master immediately chimed in, “I believe you!”

In modern terms, the Phoenix Master was practically a die-hard fan of the Celestial Thearch.

“Thank you for your trust, Phoenix Immortal.” The Celestial Thearch smiled and added, “But I don’t even believe myself~”

Phoenix Master’s claws trembled: “!!!”

“Well, I’m off. I’ll be back in a few days.” The Celestial Thearch thought for a moment, reached out to Song Shuhang, and snatched away his blanket, which hadn’t yet been used, draping it over herself.

After wrapping the blanket around herself, she dispelled the illusion on her body.

“Where are you going?” the Scarlet Heaven Sword asked, puzzled.

The Celestial Thearch: “Like I said, I’m going to cut Cheng Lin.”

“Uh-huh. Do you even know where Cheng Lin is?” the Scarlet Heaven Sword questioned.

The Celestial Thearch: “Don’t worry... I have a lead.”

With that, the Celestial Thearch kicked her long legs into the void, opened a spatial gate, and disappeared.

The Scarlet Heaven Sword: “...”

After some thought, it contacted Daoist Scarlet Heaven.

Scarlet Heaven: “???”

What kind of weird nickname is ‘Ashao’?

The Scarlet Heaven Sword explained, [I noticed that Fairy Sound Bamboo calls Shuhang ‘Ashu’ so affectionately, so I figured I’d change things up. But if I called you ‘Achi,’ it’d sound like an insult. So, I went with ‘Ashao.’]

Scarlet Heaven: “...”

[Anyway, on a serious note, Ashao, the Celestial Thearch is going to cut Cheng Lin. You might want to warn Cheng Lin to be careful.] The Scarlet Heaven Sword advised.

Daoist Scarlet Heaven thought for a moment and said, “Why don’t you just tell the Celestial Thearch that Cheng Lin has gone to the mysterious island?”

The Scarlet Heaven Sword: [???]

Isn’t that selling out your teammate?

“The truth is, Cheng Lin has also been looking for the Celestial Thearch. If the Celestial Thearch wants to cut Cheng Lin, it’ll fulfill both of their wishes. Isn’t that perfect?” Daoist Scarlet Heaven replied.

The Scarlet Heaven Sword: [That actually makes a lot of sense.]

But by now, the Celestial Thearch was already gone.

...

...

Meanwhile, in the temporary chat group Song Shuhang was part of.

“Fairy Cheng Lin, do you think you can handle the Celestial Thearch?” Senior White casually asked.

He knew Fairy Cheng Lin had been keeping tabs on Song Shuhang’s situation, so she was undoubtedly aware of the Celestial Thearch’s resurrection.

“Not really, but it doesn’t matter, Senior White... I’ve already died more than once.” Fairy Cheng Lin replied, “Besides, the Celestial Thearch looking for Fairy Cheng Lin has nothing to do with me, Cheng Goudan. Who’s Cheng Lin anyway? Never heard of her.”

“Good to hear.” Senior White responded calmly.

Members of the “Nine Provinces Number One Group” had a knack for maintaining composure during the wildest of conversations.

“By the way, Song Shuhang, how are you holding up?” Fairy Cheng Lin asked.

After taking a strike from the Celestial Thearch, his physical body was frozen in place, unable to move. It was unclear if his consciousness was still communicative.

[System Alert: Tyrannical Song has crashed... Please try again later.]

“You’ve crashed again? Not to be harsh, but you really need to upgrade your hardware to keep up with the times.” Fairy Cheng Lin remarked.

But at that moment, Song Shuhang was unable to respond.

Under the influence of the Celestial Thearch’s “Sword of Time—Fleeting Clouds, Flowing Water for Ten Years,” he realized that his signal seemed to be syncing with another signal from the void.

The reason they were syncing was because both signals originated from the same source.

One was Song Shuhang’s own signal, while the other... transcended the myriad realms, existing high above the heavens.

Chapter 2959: Comprehension: Quasi Heavenly Dao Smashing Books

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

The Emperor’s sword was meant to make whoever was struck by it experience the ravages of time all at once, effectively accelerating the aging process to the point where they’d show symptoms of dementia.

After being hit by that sword, Song Shuhang’s consciousness began to drift.

At that moment, his spiritual awareness split into two.

One part synchronized with the Sage’s Eye, which received data from the Heavenly Emperor, refining and relaying it back to Song Shuhang.

The other part, influenced by the power of time, floated higher and higher, like he was intoxicated.

Song Shuhang felt like his mind was clear, but he couldn’t control his drifting spiritual awareness.

After floating for a few seconds, the power of time, influenced by the “Age Sword,” served as a bridge that connected Song Shuhang’s consciousness with that of another “Song Shuhang” from a different frequency.

——It was the “Old Tyrant Song” attached to Daozi’s back!

Seconds later.

Song Shuhang entered a familiar “dreaming” state.

But this time, it was different from the past.

This time, the “dreaming” was actually a “dream within a dream.”

And the subject of this “dream within a dream” was none other than Daozi.

The entry point into this dream was when Daozi ascended to become the 8.5th Heavenly Dao!

—

—

Within the dream.

Daozi floated at the connection point between the Core World and the real world.

Below was the “Ancient Heavenly Court Fragment,” fused with the Core World, and the “Heavenly Emperor’s Dao” was attached to Daozi.

Song Shuhang’s vision synchronized with Daozi as he ascended to become a Heavenly Dao.

As soon as they synchronized in the dream, Song Shuhang vaguely sensed Daozi’s subconscious resistance — true experts possess the ability to perceive through time and space, and they could sense Song Shuhang’s “dreaming” state.

Daozi, who was in the process of ascending to the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, was indeed a true expert among experts. Naturally, he could sense Song Shuhang’s presence.

However, that resistance was only momentary. Then, Daozi began to cooperate, even going so far as to open his state of mind to Song Shuhang.

Clearly, Daozi had recognized Song Shuhang’s identity.

Song Shuhang had strong ties to the Confucian Sage, Yunquezi, the thirteen Confucian Tribulation Immortals, the Fairy of Creation, the Golden Lotus World, and Venerable Henghuo — though despite these connections, he was destined never to become a part of the Confucian sect.

After recognizing Song Shuhang’s identity, Daozi, under the circumstances, naturally opened the door for him.

This shows how important connections are in cultivation.

With strong enough connections, even the Heavenly Dao could endorse you, share their glory and experiences, and maybe even help you ascend.

Within the dream.

Song Shuhang’s “vision” was synchronized with Daozi’s as he sat on the Emperor’s Throne, slowly ascending while overlooking the myriad worlds.

The view of the Heavenly Dao encompassed all worlds in an instant.

Among them, Song Shuhang recognized Earth, then the Beast Realm, the Dream World, the realm of the creditor “Shadow Lord,” and finally, his “Tyrant World.”

After scanning these, Song Shuhang — or rather, Daozi’s — gaze landed on Su Clan’s Sixteen.

Previously, Su Clan’s Sixteen had lowered her own tribulation to assist Daozi’s plan to ascend as the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, lending him a hand.

So, naturally, after Daozi’s ascension, he had to repay this favor.

As an ascending Heavenly Dao, all Daozi needed to do was glance at Su Clan’s Sixteen, and the thought of gratitude would cause the laws of the myriad worlds to respond.

A surge of power, akin to what one would receive after giving a “Saintly Lecture,” fell upon Su Clan’s Sixteen, enhancing her luck and merit.

The merit from an ordinary Saintly Lecture wasn’t particularly strong. Every time Song Shuhang lectured, the merit he gained was several times that of a regular Saintly Lecture.

However, the merit Su Clan’s Sixteen received was just the beginning. Once Daozi fully ascended, that merit would increase several times over.

Helping the Heavenly Dao ascend is equivalent to achieving “功德无量” (boundless merit), and the merit that comes from this is immeasurable.

Moreover, the merit itself isn’t the most important part.

The most important part is the “Heavenly Dao’s gratitude” contained within the merit — essentially, it’s a powerful buff.

From now on, every time Su Clan’s Sixteen faces a tribulation, the Heavenly Tribulation will acknowledge this buff and give her a pass.

After seeing this, Song Shuhang felt a sense of relief deep in his heart.

With this, Su Clan’s Sixteen would no longer need to worry about future tribulations. Even after Daozi steps down as the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, this buff will remain in effect.

Unless the next Heavenly Dao bears a grudge against Daozi and deliberately cancels this “Heavenly Dao’s buff.”

After settling Su Clan’s Sixteen’s karma, Daozi continued to ascend from the throne.

During this time... the attached Song Shuhang vaguely heard a voice in his ear.

This seemed to be the scene where “Old Tyrant Song” whispered into Daozi’s ear.

Song Shuhang couldn’t make out what “Old Tyrant Song” was saying.

However, he wasn’t in a hurry to find out. After all, he would be the one saying it in the future, so there was nothing to be curious about.

After finishing his whisper, Daozi suddenly exploded with rage, shattering the void with a book.

In the dream, from a first-person perspective, Song Shuhang clearly sensed Daozi’s technique of smashing the void with the Confucian Scriptures!

*I wonder if I could pull that off too?* Song Shuhang thought, his mind suddenly racing.

When Daozi shattered the void, he was still in the process of becoming a Heavenly Dao, in a proto-Heavenly Dao state. At the moment, Song Shuhang’s main body possessed the “Immortal Fat Whale Golden Core” plus the “pseudo-immortal mode.”

The two were worlds apart in terms of power, but their statuses bore some similarities.

Song Shuhang carefully replayed every step of Daozi’s move in his mind, simulating it...

A few moments later, taking advantage of the “dreaming” state, he successfully grasped an attack technique — “Proto-Heavenly Dao Book Smash!”

This is a temporary name.

Later, he would change the name to something more like the Heavenly Emperor’s “Age Sword,” enhancing its gravitas.

With the Confucian Scriptures he now held, should he ever face a formidable enemy, he could unleash a proto-Heavenly Dao level book smash attack right to the face!

As he pondered, Daozi in the dream had already obliterated the “Void Guardian” and the “Stellar Doom.”

Daozi continued to ascend.

Finally, he officially made contact with the “Heavenly Dao.”

The immortal laws began to reshape Daozi.

*Boom!*

In an instant, the dream-state Song Shuhang felt like his brain was about to explode.

The “Immortal Fat Whale Golden Core” in his life-bound dantian swelled like a pufferfish, vigorously bouncing.

In a split second, Song Shuhang’s consciousness elevated to an unprecedented height.

His vision exceeded the limitations of the myriad worlds, rising above all immortal beings!

Chapter 2960: Deriving the Path to Immortality, If Not Now, When?

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

In an instant... a moment so brief it’s impossible to describe, a time so short that for a normal person, it’s not even enough to form a single thought.

But for an entity of “Heavenly Dao” level, an instant is enough to accomplish countless tasks!

In this fleeting moment, Song Shuhang’s perception and thoughts were elevated to their absolute limits.

Thus, in this moment, his inner monologue could become extraordinarily rich.

He could compress countless thoughts into this “instant” and complete them!

At this moment, time for Song Shuhang had nearly come to a standstill!

—

—

[So, this is the data of the Heavenly Dao?]

As Song Shuhang entered the dream of the “Dao Child,” coming into contact with the Heavenly Dao and condensing an immortal body, he couldn’t quite believe it.

The secrets of the Heavenly Dao are the greatest mysteries in the universe. Even when a fragment is revealed, it’s only the tip of an immense iceberg.

Yet now, he had touched the essence of that iceberg.

Although his mind felt like it would explode upon contact, he had indeed accessed the core secrets of the Heavenly Dao through the “Dao Child.”

[To think I could even access this information in a dream!]

If he could tap into the core secrets of the Heavenly Dao in a dream, then there was nothing in the myriad worlds that he, Ba Song, couldn’t access!

From borrowing books, cheating the tribulation, borrowing laws, life experiences, karma, merits, and bosses, Ba Song had endured hardships to finally reach the ultimate secret of the universe.

Fortunately... his foundation was solid!

If he didn’t have the “Immortal Whale Golden Core” in his body, if he didn’t have the golden dragon pattern on his core that Senior White Two had drawn with Heavenly Dao authority, if he hadn’t experienced a “pseudo-immortal state,” or if he hadn’t repeatedly encountered “Heavenly Dao information” in the past... then in the moment he tapped into the Dao Child’s ascension to Heavenly Dao, he would have been utterly destroyed, both in body and soul!

Even if he were to be revived, he would have ended up in eternal slumber, much like the “Undying Lord” of old.

Luckily, his past accumulations had laid the most solid foundation for this moment of “accessing the core secrets of the Heavenly Dao”!

Additionally, his strong pain tolerance allowed him to maintain his thoughts even in the excruciating pain that felt like his brain was about to melt!

And as long as he could maintain some semblance of clear thinking, he could accomplish a great deal in that “instant.”

For example, deriving the “Path to Immortality”!

The information on the two paths to immortality within Song Shuhang’s body was already partially understood. Although he hadn’t fully grasped the “principle of immortality,” he could steadily advance toward the “Immortal” realm and achieve a state of “neither life nor death” as long as he followed the steps. Even if he didn’t fully understand it, the formula was already established; as long as his body followed the formula, the correct answer would naturally emerge.

The other path, related to the “Cultivation Chat System,” required a perspective far beyond that of an ordinary cultivator, one that looked down on the myriad worlds from the pinnacle.

[So, it’s now or never!] Song Shuhang focused all his remaining energy on deducing the “Cultivation Chat System’s Path to Immortality.”

Whether or not he succeeded, this was his only option at the moment!

If not now, then when?

Everything within Song Shuhang was mobilized, contributing to the deduction of the “Cultivation Chat System’s Path to Immortality.”

Compared to the “Neither Life nor Death Path to Immortality,” the “Cultivation Chat System’s Path to Immortality” was the true path that integrated all his potential into one grand avenue.

The 7+1 core, the super Heavenly Dao-level golden dragon pattern that Senior White Two had drawn, the star map on the golden core, the seven saint seals + world master seal, the law of root characters, the law of Hua Bei, the power of karma, the merit network, the immortal whale golden core, the pseudo-immortal body, the Cultivation Chat System—all these unique abilities of Song Shuhang converged at this moment!

The “Neither Life nor Death Path to Immortality” represented Song Shuhang’s singular specialty in the aspect of death.

The “Cultivation Chat System’s Path to Immortality” was the grand avenue that fully realized all of Song Shuhang’s attributes!

—

—

In the real world.

“Huh?” Pavilion Master Chu’s hair strand blinked in surprise.

Because suddenly, she sensed that Song Shuhang’s head had heated up to a terrifying degree, hot enough to burn even an immortal.

Moreover...

In that brief moment, she vaguely sensed that Song Shuhang’s body was constantly collapsing and reforming!

“Eighty times? Or ninety? Or maybe even more?” Pavilion Master Chu’s hair strand couldn’t calculate the exact number in that instant.

She only knew that after Song Shuhang’s head began to heat up, his body reached a critical point where it couldn’t bear the strain and started collapsing.

However, today, the “Immortal Whale Golden Core” within Song Shuhang seemed to have found a source of endless energy, continuously charging.

Each time Song Shuhang’s body collapsed, the Immortal Whale Golden Core immediately restored it.

This cycle repeated eighty or ninety times, perhaps even more—possibly over a hundred.

In that brief instant, Song Shuhang’s death count might have increased by three digits.

This was truly the act of burning with life.

“So hot!” Phoenix Claw also cried out, perched on Song Shuhang’s head. “What’s happening? The Heavenly Emperor’s ‘Dementia Sword’ didn’t have a head-heating effect, did it?”

“It’s probably not the Heavenly Emperor’s ‘Dementia Sword.’ That strike might have served as a trigger, guiding Song Shuhang into a deeper transformation,” the Stone Tablet Spirit said slowly.

As Ba Song’s tombstone, it always observed him with a unique perspective.

“For just a moment... there was a trace of Heavenly Dao,” Senior White Two’s voice sounded, crossing the channel between the “Evil Lotus World” and the “Core World.”

As soon as Senior White Two’s voice echoed, the “liquid metal windbreaker” on Song Shuhang’s back fluttered without wind.

The windbreaker was particularly sensitive to this voice!

It felt a deep-rooted loathing for this voice... yet in the deepest recesses of its core, it also felt a certain attachment, an unwillingness to part with this voice, or perhaps envy towards its owner.

In short, its emotions were very complicated.

After fluttering for a moment, the windbreaker calmed down again—it was just an avatar, and now was the time to focus on the main body’s condition.

“The main body is indeed accessing ‘Heavenly Dao’ information.” The windbreaker also spoke, “And I can confirm that the main body is likely retrieving his own power. I can sense a familiar scent in the ‘Heavenly Dao information’ he’s accessing—a scent that belonged to my main body in the past!”

Senior White Two was speechless.

Just by listening to the voice, Senior White Two could detect a strong sense of “pride” in Ball Shuhang’s tone.

Senior White Two’s gaze shifted again to the Nine Nether World, where a black metal mass had condensed to the size of a fist in its source.

He couldn’t wait to see the scene when Ball Shuhang finally revived!

Senior White Two eagerly anticipated the emergence of “Fatty • Pufferfish • Ball.”

Chapter 2961: Gentle Immortal Yuelun

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Just imagining Fat Ball getting so mad that it puffs up, sprouting spikes all over its round body, made White Senior Two incredibly amused.

He was curious just how big Fat Ball would get when it puffed up with spikes. If a small pufferfish can swell to the size of a little ball, then Fat Ball, in proportion, might expand to the size of a village-level grenade. Or maybe even larger—county-level? City-level?

As the ruler of the Netherworld, White Senior Two realized that to live happily, he needed a worthy opponent, someone who could occasionally bring him joy.

In the past, White Senior Two found Fat Ball quite annoying at times—but now that Fat Ball had truly revived, White Senior Two found himself oddly pleased.

“Senior Song has stopped heating up,” Black-Skinned Soft Feather, who was always attentive, pointed out.

The heat radiating from Tyrannical Song’s head had begun to dissipate, and his body was no longer disintegrating and regenerating.

The tuft of hair on Pavilion Master Chu’s head swayed elegantly as she cast a water-based healing spell, gently covering Song Shuhang’s head.

The healing spell from the Clear Water Pavilion was subtle yet effective, like a gentle mist enveloping him.

As it settled on his head, a faint “ssssss” sound was heard, and a soft white mist rose.

“Is he waking up?” asked the Red Cloud Sword.

Stele Daoist replied, “It doesn’t seem like it.”

Black-Skinned Feathered Soft Child explained, “Senior Red Cloud Sword, those are actually the Sage’s Eyes, processing information. That’s why he looks alert. You should check out his Third Eye instead; it doesn’t seem to be focused.”

“I tried to @-mention Shuhang in the Cultivation Chat System, but it says he’s still in a shutdown state,” White Senior Two’s voice chimed in. “It seems he’s latched onto something truly extraordinary this time.”
