“Fairy @#%×, you take care of Shuhang from here on out,” White Senior Two instructed.

The Merit Snake Beauty slowly coiled around Song Shuhang, using the power of merit to nurture his body.

The painful expression on Song Shuhang’s face eased, and the frown on his brow softened.

In the dream.

The Daoist had successfully completed the ritual, becoming the 8.5th Heavenly Dao.

At that moment, the Daoist had started to familiarize himself with the “Heavenly Dao Authority,” experimenting with using its rules and powers on a small scale.

Meanwhile, Song Shuhang finally emerged from that brain-melting state of deduction.

The aftereffects of that single moment of intense mental strain were overwhelming.

Even now, Song Shuhang’s brain remained in a daze. Although he was in the dream, attached to the Daoist’s body, he could only numbly sense the Daoist’s manipulation of the Heavenly Dao Authority. His foggy mind couldn’t comprehend any insights.

His brain was utterly exhausted.

This immense opportunity—personally experiencing the operation of the Heavenly Dao Authority—was something Song Shuhang could barely take advantage of in his current state.

Sometimes in life, you can’t have both the fish and the bear paw; you have to make a choice.

But fortunately, Song Shuhang didn’t feel any regret.

Because—besides him, there was also the “Old Tyrant Song!”

While he might not be able to seize this chance to experience the Heavenly Dao’s power, it didn’t mean he wouldn’t have another opportunity in the future. The “Old Tyrant Song” from the future would relive this moment anyway.

If you can’t have both fish and bear paw, then this time, I’ll have the fish, and next time, I’ll have the bear paw!

In the dream, the Daoist continued to familiarize himself with the Heavenly Dao Authority and began devising a plan to resolve the aftereffects of the Confucian disciples’ resurrection.

Meanwhile, Song Shuhang’s dazed mind slowly started to recover.

The mental exertion from that single moment was vast, but the rewards were equally significant!

Firstly... Song Shuhang had fully comprehended the “Non-Life, Non-Death Path to Immortality.”

This was an unexpected gain.

Song Shuhang had been using that brief moment of Heavenly Dao insight to deduce the “Cultivation Chat Immortal Path” and hadn’t intended to delve into the “Non-Life, Non-Death Path.”

After all, the framework for the “Non-Life, Non-Death Path to Immortality” had already been established, and it would unfold naturally.

But as he worked on the “Cultivation Chat Immortal Path,” his understanding of the “Non-Life, Non-Death Path” deepened.

Both paths were carved from his own body, both were his paths to immortality... so, naturally, they weren’t entirely separate.

The two immortal paths shared many commonalities, influencing and complementing each other. Gaining a deeper understanding of one also enhanced his understanding of the other.

As Song Shuhang had predicted, the “Non-Life, Non-Death Path to Immortality” was an extreme and brutal path to immortality.

Its extremity and brutality weren’t directed at others—but at Song Shuhang himself!

“It does have some similarities to Fairy Cheng Lin’s ‘dead as can be’ state, but they are fundamentally opposite.”

Fairy Cheng Lin’s path to immortality was the “Path of Birthing New Life.” She would give birth to a new version of herself periodically, shedding the old self in a process that made her stronger, shedding death, and achieving endless life.

Song Shuhang’s current “Non-Life, Non-Death Path to Immortality” was also a cyclical path, similar to Fairy Cheng Lin’s, with a transformation occurring after each cycle.

However, while Fairy Cheng Lin’s transformation leaned towards life, Song Shuhang’s path leaned towards death.

After each cycle, the “Non-Life, Non-Death Path to Immortality” would experience death, during which all negative effects would be “killed off,” followed by rebirth... In this way, the revived Tyrant Song would become stronger than before.

And typically, both Tyrant Song and Fairy Cheng Lin existed in a peculiar “Non-Life, Non-Death” state.

One cycle led towards life, while the other towards death.

“Non-Life, Non-Death is just a state of this immortal path... This path seeks life through death,” Song Shuhang murmured.

This was the counterpart to Fairy Cheng Lin’s “Path of Birthing New Life”: the “Path of Seeking Life Through Death.”

As Song Shuhang fully comprehended this immortal path, his physical body in the real world began to undergo a corresponding transformation.

The Realm of Three Corpses Calamity Immortal, in the Primordial Era, was also known as the “Weak Immortal Realm.”

If a Calamity Immortal in this realm truly grasped an immortal path, they would immediately attain the Way.

And now, the same was happening with Song Shuhang.

As he achieved enlightenment, a moon wheel quietly appeared behind his head.

Its glow was as gentle as water.

Though the “Non-Life, Non-Death Path to Immortality” was a harsh and extreme path towards immortality, the light of this moon wheel was incredibly gentle, revealing a rare, tender brilliance.

The soft glow illuminated the tuft of hair on Lord Chu’s head and shone upon Phoenix Claw’s paws...

It also bathed all of Song Shuhang’s nearby companions in its light.

Phoenix Claw stared blankly at the glow for a moment before blurting out, “Youyou!”

Chapter 2965: Chapter 2963: Shuhang Everywhere

[In this way, if Tyrannical Song wants to compete for the Ninth Heavenly Dao, his foundation will be even more solid.] Daozi slightly smiles, staying modest about his accomplishment and fame.

Main world.

The Eight-Armed Primordial Cosmic Demon displayed a smile of relief on its face, repeatedly mumbling several phrases in ancient language.

It should be words similar to ‘it’s so good.’

After mumbling for quite a while, it too turned around and bowed in the direction of Song Shuhang’s main body.

“From this moment, the curse laid upon our race by the Fourth Heavenly Dao has finally dissipated. Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, I will etch this kindness deeply in my heart. After this affair, should Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song wish to prove his Dao and become immortal, I am willing to serve loyally before and after the horse.” The leader of the Eight-Armed Outer Heavenly Demon spoke out.

Chapter 2967: Chapter 2965: The Will of the Heavens Takes You Flying!
The eight-armed cosmic demon grandee was indebted to Tyrannical Song for a favor—he was in an exceptionally good mood after witnessing Tyrannical Song assist “Daozi” in removing the curse on the cosmic demon clan. Looking towards Song Shuhang’s position, he made a promise.

Someday, if Tyrannical Song intended to compete for the Heavenly Dao, he was willing to lend him a helping hand!

After all, the eight-armed cosmic demon himself had no intention of competing for the Heavenly Dao. Partly because he had been through much, and partly because of the curse laid upon his cosmic demon clan.

Since he harbored no thoughts of contending for the Heavenly Dao, if the next Heavenly Dao was on good terms with their cosmic demon clan, that would be a great choice!

At least, they wouldn’t have to worry about their cosmic demon clan being targeted again.

After the voice of the eight-armed cosmic demon grandee fell, a “Heaven and Earth Phenomenon” manifested in the vacuum, descending upon him and Tyrannical Song.

Golden mythical beasts danced around the eight-armed cosmic demon, becoming the carrier of the “promise”!

—This was the Heaven and Earth Phenomenon caused by the witnessing of the Heavenly Dao.

Seeing the eight-armed cosmic demon voluntarily coming forward, becoming the assistant for Tyrannical Song in the competition for the next Heavenly Dao, Daozi naturally took the opportunity to secure this “assistant”!

Like the thought of the cosmic demon from the eight domains, Daozi also felt that if the next Heavenly Dao was Tyrannical Song, who was on good terms with Confucianism, it would be a very good choice.

Thus, there would be no need to worry about Confucianism being targeted again.

Under a mutual agreement, this promise was witnessed by the Heavenly Dao and spread to the myriad practitioners in the universe.

All cultivators in the myriad practitioners in the universe were moved again.

Today, everyone had been forced to experience heart movement multiple times; in fact, their hearts had become slightly numb.

Summing up this “Heavenly Dao witnessing”... in the future, if Tyrannical Song were to compete for the next Heavenly Dao, the cultivators of the myriad practitioners in the universe, apart from having to defeat “fat ball Song” first, might also have to challenge the eight-armed cosmic demon grandee before having a shot at challenging Tyrannical Song.

Utterly merciless, giving no chance to others!

However, some perceptive grandees suddenly noticed something— the newly incumbent Heavenly Dao was actually witnessing the oath for “the eight-armed cosmic demon assisting Tyrannical Song in competing for the next Heavenly Dao.”

This was indeed intriguing!

Could it be that the freshly appointed “Heavenly Dao” had already decided when to “retire successfully”? Was he secretly designating “Tyrannical Song” as the next Heavenly Dao candidate?

Was the seat of the Heavenly Dao about to become hereditary?

What undisclosed secret negotiations existed between Tyrannical Song and the new Heavenly Dao “Daozi”?

What secrets lay hidden behind the succession of each generation’s “Immortal Heavenly Dao”?

Had Tyrannical Song and the new Heavenly Dao deciphered this secret and conspired to alternate in proving their Dao to immortality, cycling through the Heavenly Dao seat, and then transferring the seat of the Heavenly Dao to other fellow friends?

At that moment, some of the top immortals among the myriad realms had thousands of thoughts—tonight, this group of top immortals would probably find it hard to sleep.

...

In the main world.

After making the promise, the eight-armed cosmic demon grandee closely sensed Tyrannical Song’s location and his condition.

The eight-armed cosmic demon grandee tossed the elixir towards Song Shuhang’s position.

—He had just sensed that Song Shuhang had collaborated with “Daozi” to incarnate thousands to lift the curse on the cosmic demon clan and had then fallen into extreme weakness.

Therefore, the eight-armed cosmic demon grandee sent over this precious elixir, the effects of which were similar to the twice-filtered “Void Sun Guardians” absorbed by Song Shuhang.

The elixirs containing ‘Immortality Material’ could be refined during the ancient times, but nowadays they can hardly be produced... unless one were to kill an Immortal and offer it to the heavens?

After handing over the small jade box, the Eight-Armed Outer Heavenly Demon let out a deep sigh of relief as if he had set down an enormous burden.

His figure merged into the giant statue, temporarily lurking.

Song Shuhang’s location.

“Is it over?” Black-skinned Soft Feather looked up and asked.

Senior White two pondered for a moment and guessed, “It seems that Shuhang wants to take this opportunity to completely perfect his second path to immortality.”

He could sense that the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ was continuously upgrading in the background.

Once the second path to immortality was completely perfected, there was no need to step out immediately, but it could be used as a backup path like the original Heavenly Emperor.

Should the currently proven ‘Seeking Life Through Death Path to Immortality’ that Song Shuhang has dissipate, the backup path of immortality could be activated immediately!

...

In the dream plot.

“Thank you, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, for lending me a hand,” Daozi said with a smile.

Song Shuhang replied, “Daozi senior brother, it is clearly I who benefitted here, I should be thanking you.”

“Mutual benefit,” Daozi said tiredly, sitting on the throne, “Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, I saw you deducing a vast path to immortality in a ‘moment’ earlier?”

Even Daozi, who was an 8.5 Tier Heavenly Dao, felt that the path to immortality was ‘vast’, almost equal to the Confucian Dao developed by his teacher.

The path to immortality of the Confucian sage was enormous and comprehensive, and within it, many branches of the path to immortality could even extend, each providing the thirteen Tribulation Transcenders of Confucianism with an opportunity to ‘prove their Dao’.

“Indeed, that is my second method to immortality. But this method is too vast, beyond the vision of ordinary immortals to perfect,” replied Song Shuhang.

Even using ‘Dark Song’s ruler of the Netherworld privileges seemed insufficient to complete it.

Song Shuhang, using the moment of ‘Great Way Light Wheel’ status, did gain a lot of insights... but it was still short of being completely perfected.

That is to say, the path to immortality related to the ‘Cultivator Chat System’, its vastness was such that even the Heavenly Dao could not perfect it in a ‘moment’!

“Then, how about I lend a hand to Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song?” Daozi responded.

With his friend’s obsessions resolved and the redemptions to be fulfilled already completed, now was Daozi’s brief rest period.

“Daozi senior brother, would you help me deduce the path to immortality?” Song Shuhang’s eyes brightened.

“The path to immortality is best deduced by oneself,” Daozi said with a slight smile, “I can assist you from the side. First... let us broaden our horizons, and from the perspective of the Heavenly Dao, observe the myriad practitioners in the universe.”

The path to immortality, after all, is a very personal affair.

Upon saying this, Daozi pressed his hands before his eyes.

Song Shuhang’s visual perspective synchronized with Daozi’s.

The next moment, every realm and every detail of the myriad practitioners in the universe appeared before Song Shuhang’s eyes.

The explosion of data nearly burst Song Shuhang’s head!

Chapter 2968: Chapter 2966: You Are Courting Death!
However, with the Scholarly Sage’s Eye diligently protecting Song Shuhang,

there was no chance for Song Shuhang’s head to explode.

At this moment, all the planes of the myriad practitioners in the universe appeared in Song Shuhang’s eyes simultaneously, in a manner of overlapping lines.

This type of vision far surpassed the concept of optical vision; it was an impact that came from the depths of the soul!

The immense shock immediately caused terms like “Holy cow, awesome, truly magnificent, incredible” and such to flood Shuhang’s mind...

The impact of the visuals was so intense that it caused Song Shuhang to lose all the words he had accumulated over more than a decade of education—to the extent that they seemed sent off to Wa Claw Country!

Apart from terms like ‘Holy cow, awesome,’ for a moment, he couldn’t squeeze out any more appropriate idioms.

Perhaps once he calmed down a bit, he could think of some fitting phrases...

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, calm down and thoroughly experience this myriad world. Viewing the world from the Heavenly Dao’s perspective should be of some help to you... Huh?” While speaking, Daozi suddenly paused.

He seemed to have sensed something!

At the same time, Song Shuhang, through Daozi’s viewpoint, noticed what he had focused on.

—Among the myriad big and small planes of the universe, there were countless light points.

Those were the myriad stars of the universe.

Under the gaze of Daozi, the secrets hidden within the stars could not be obscured and were seen through in a glance.

“Is this the Stellar Destruction Virus?” Daozi asked aloud.

He had recently learned a bit about the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus,’ ‘Virtual Sun Guardians,’ and ‘Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull’ through his interaction with Tyrannical Song.

However, he had not expected the virus to have spread to such an exaggerated extent!

In the myriad stars of the universe, at least over 60% were densely infected by the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus,’ causing a tingling sensation on Daozi’s scalp.

This was a method capable of destroying ‘all the realms of the universe,’ a catastrophe of unprecedented magnitude!

If these ‘Stellar Destruction Viruses’ were activated, no one in all the realms would escape... not even the ‘world of the golden lotus’ knew if it could survive this calamity!

“[I just managed to erase the ‘Resurrection Aftereffect’ for my junior brothers, and just managed to complete my own obsession, and now you want to play out a ‘world doomsday’ plot?]”

At this moment, Daozi’s heart was filled with anger and irritation.

You are courting death!

“Yes, that’s them.” Song Shuhang replied.

He too felt his scalp tingle and his hair stand on end.

From Fat Ball Song’s investigation, Song Shuhang had obtained some data on the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus.’

But, merely the numbers were nothing compared to the visual impact he saw with his eyes.

This was similar to the principle of how exhilarating credit card spending is... when you’re only swiping numbers, it’s different from actually paying with money.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, you observ carefully this myriad realms, I need to recuperate a bit.” Daozi said solemnly.

After all, he was only a supplementary 0.5 part of Heavenly Dao, and there were still differences from the true Heavenly Dao. Thus, after completing his obsession with Song Eldest and the Eight-Armed Outer Heavenly Demon in one breath, he was a bit exhausted. If he wanted to create big news, he needed to recuperate a bit.

At the same time, he also needed to temporarily familiarize himself with the Heavenly Dao’s laws that would be ‘targeted against the Stellar Destruction Virus’.

During this period, Daozi completely shared the ‘Heavenly Dao’s view’ with Song Shuhang, allowing him to stand in the spectator mode’ perspective and view the world through the eyes of the Heavenly Dao.

All things were in sight, and everything in the world seemed to be under control.

This is the Heavenly Dao!

...

At the location of Song Shuhang’s main body.

The Scholarly Sage’s Eye was frantically engaged in calculation, and this time, even the third eye joined in, lightening the computational burden on the Scholarly Sage’s eyes.

In the dream, Song Shuhang’s vision split into two different states.

He could pay attention to the entire myriad realms simultaneously and could also lock onto certain detailed parts to observe closely.

This was where his magnificent cultivation career had begun.

Here, he had met Soft Feather, Sixteen, Senior Medicine Master, and Doudou and even picked up Senior White who was coming out of secluded meditation!

Now, after experiencing the incident with evil spirits and the eruption of the world’s spiritual qi tide, Jiangnan College Town had also changed.

The evil spirits on modern world-Earth were completely exterminated by the demons of the Ninth Stage sent by Song Shuhang, the disaster was over.

However, the rejuvenating spiritual power added an extra touch of fantasy to the world.

At this time, Jiangnan College Town was sparsely populated.

Not because it was abandoned, but because ... it was winter break!

“Winter break, I always feel it’s a very distant term,” Song Shuhang reflected inwardly.

It felt so close yet so far away.

Song Shuhang’s gaze swept over Jiangnan College Town.

Even during winter break, there were still some members lingering in the school.

It seems that Jiangnan College might add a few special classes next semester?

Senior White’s pet, monster willow Soft Feather, was still rooted in Jiangnan College Town.

Song Shuhang’s gaze locked onto her—monster willow Soft Feather had always been attending school on his behalf, covering for him.

Afterward, he must not treat her unfairly.

Should he talk to Senior White and raise her benefits?

The monster willow Soft Feather also felt a movement in her heart, as if being watched, she lifted her branches, turning around in puzzlement.

But the observation of the Heavenly Dao, she truly could not sense anything.

So, she swayed her branches, stretched out a pair of little hands from her trunk, took out her phone, opened the chat app, and pulled up a group chat.

The group name was “Lifelong Good Buddies.”

Inside were Tubo, Gao Moumou, Yang De ... and Soft Feather.

Song Shuhang himself, however, wasn’t in the group!!

Suddenly, he had a feeling of being abandoned by his good buddies.

Song Shuhang’s gaze then swept over Soft Feather’s chat history.

Immediately afterward, he discovered that his three roommates were asking Soft Feather about cultivation issues.

It must have been the safety net left by Song Shuhang that worked, combined with the incident involving evil spirits and the rejuvenation of the world’s spiritual power, his three roommates were completely convinced about the existence of cultivation.

Monster willow Soft Feather, with a hobby of “fostering salted fish roommates,” began to guide them in cultivation.

For now, Soft Feather was gradually turning Song Shuhang’s three roommates into housebound cultivators, who only knew to remain in secluded cultivation at home every day.

Song Shuhang: “...”

The matter with his three roommates could be put aside for now.

When the calamity of the world’s end was resolved, when everything was over, he could free up his hands to truly help them.

For now, it was fine letting Soft Feather take care of them.

Then, Song Shuhang’s gaze swept over the Immortal Farming Sect, Chuchu’s home, and the sea urchin warrior clan at the bottom of the ocean.

He was scanning familiar places one by one, according to the events he had experienced in his memories.

A moment later, Song Shuhang’s eyes grazed over the mysterious island!

On the mysterious island, he saw a golden Cheng Lin, standing in front of The White Dragon’s dragon tomb.

“Eh?” Song Shuhang’s eyes suddenly brightened.

Chapter 2969: Chapter 2967: Obviously, You’re Not the One I’ve Been Mainly Waiting for!
Golden Tranquil.

But it was not Cheng Lin!

Song Shuhang knew Cheng Goudan all too well.

Although Cheng Goudan wasn’t like Chu Pavilion Lord’s Dumb Hair, Fairy Creation, or @#%× Fairy, stuck on Song Shuhang, Cheng Goudan had always been one of Song Shuhang’s distant cheats and also a bridge between Song Shuhang and Father Goudan.

Therefore, even though this golden Cheng Lin looked almost exactly like Cheng Lin and had a very similar demeanor, Song Shuhang could tell at a glance that this Cheng Lin wasn’t that Cheng Lin.

Moreover, Song Shuhang was currently observing the mortal world through “Heavenly Dao’s Vision.”

Golden Tranquil stood calmly in front of the dragon tomb’s “crystal coffin,” her right hand gently pressed on the coffin, seemingly whispering something.

Above the dragon tomb, a silver-haired fairy with a scar on her back and a bald fairy stood side by side, seemingly watching the changes occurring within the dragon tomb.

Not far above the mysterious island, the resurrected Heavenly Emperor, wrapped in a sheet and barefoot in the vacuum, overlooked the mysterious island but did not attack right away, seeming to stand there observing.

In the vacuum not far from the mysterious island, the figure of a great lord shimmered in and out of visibility — the aura emanating from this great lord bore some resemblance to that of Senior Copper Trigram from the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

Further away, two figures were rapidly approaching.

One was Senior Golden Trigram, who had completed his agreement with Song Woodhead and others, and the 8.5 Heavenly Dao Ceremony had ended.

Now he was hurrying back to the mysterious island.

Next, he was waiting for Daozi to fulfill their agreement and concentrate all aspects of the “Heavenly Emperor’s Path” onto him, making Golden Trigram the unique, second-generation Heavenly Emperor of the myriad practitioners in the universe.

The other was Immortal Fairy White Bones who, for some unknown reason, felt a calling and accompanied Golden Trigram in rushing back to the mysterious island.

Song Shuhang swept a glance through “Heavenly Emperor’s View” over the location of the mysterious island before returning his gaze to Golden Tranquil and that bald fairy, focusing on them.

“I was thinking of delaying our meeting a bit longer... at least until all the crises in the outside world had ended,” Golden Tranquil said softly to the crystal coffin. “But now, it seems, I do not have much time left.”

However, the White Dragon Sister was not in the dragon tomb this time and showed no signs of returning—she was still accompanying Sixteen in overcoming tribulation.

Golden Tranquil showed a beautiful smile, and like the real Cheng Lin, she adjusted her slightly skew daoist cap with her hand.

Then, she approached the ‘bloodletting slot’ of the crystal coffin.

This time, the circle of ‘ancient bronze coffins’ around the crystal coffin remained still. The Bone Dragon Artifact Spirits within them quietly awaited.

Golden Tranquil stretched out her hand and gently pulled it through the vacuum.

A large sawtoothed blade materialized in her palm.

She gripped the sawtoothed blade and began to vigorously saw her own wrist area.

Sparks flew, the teeth of the blade and her skin creating a frenzied friction and bursts of dazzling sparks.

Even under Golden Tranquil’s control, the sound of the blade sawing against her wrist started to take on a rhythm similar to that of a cello—it was Offenbach’s “Jacqueline’s Tears.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

For some reason, this scene had a taunting flavor.

It felt as if Golden Tranquil was signaling to others: Hey, little brothers, are your defenses any good? Look at mine. Golden armor, sawing with a serrated blade, sparks flying everywhere, and yet not a scratch!

Sometime after the continuous sawing, Golden Tranquil’s wrist finally breached.

From her wrist flowed a golden blood, continuously pouring into the crystal coffin’s blood slot.

Upon seeing this scene, Song Shuhang couldn’t help but think about gripping his own wrist—if it had been him, after sawing for a while with a serrated blade, his wrist would probably detach itself from the elbow. But he wouldn’t have to worry about blood.

His Tyrannical Song self, even if cut into ten or eight pieces, wouldn’t drip a single drop of blood!

That was his advantage.

Within his field of view.

Golden Tranquil’s blood filled the groove and flowed around the crystal coffin along a channel, enveloping the entire coffin layer by layer.

Exactly like the scene where Song Shuhang had his blood fill the coffin.

Golden blood traced out a beautiful formation on the crystal coffin.

The crystal coffin resonated with the golden blood.

“Is the White Dragon finally going to resurrect?” Song Shuhang thought to himself.

But moments later... the resonating golden formation dimmed again.

Golden Tranquil: “???”

She widened her eyes, incredulously staring at the small white dragon in the crystal coffin.

This was completely beyond her expectations.

“Could it be that I didn’t let enough blood?” Golden Tranquil asked.

“No, fellow friend, the blood you let was already more than enough.” From the side, the skeletal flood dragon spirit popped out its little head and spoke.

“Then, which part of the ceremony went wrong?” Golden Tranquil asked again.

The bone dragon artifact spirit: “No, there were no issues with the ceremony from start to finish.”

“Then why hasn’t she resurrected yet?” Golden Tranquil said.

“Obviously.” The bone dragon artifact spirit replied, “You are not the person my master is waiting for.”

Golden Tranquil: “...”

Song Shuhang: “...”

“Could it be a glitch in the procedure? Should I let more blood and try again?” Golden Tranquil said.

The bone dragon artifact spirit did not discount her kindness: “If you are willing, fellow friend, feel free to try as many times as you want.”

Golden Tranquil, not convinced, picked up the serrated knife and started cutting her own wrist again.

After a long while.

Golden fresh blood dripped out.

But just as the golden blood was about to drip, Golden Tranquil’s other hand swept over it, slicing through the golden elements in the blood.

The part of the blood that was golden was cut away and hovered beside her.

Then, blood with a hint of gold color fell into the groove.

The blood resonated with the crystal coffin once more!

“This time it should be settled.” Golden Tranquil patted the crystal coffin and said, “White Dragon sister, come out now, stop causing trouble. I really don’t have much time left.”

Squeak~Crack~

The crystal coffin vibrated intensely for a moment.

Then, it returned to calmness.

Golden Tranquil: “!!!”

“It failed again, fellow friend.” The bone dragon artifact spirit slowly said: “There’s no need to force it, you really are not the person my master is waiting for.”

Golden Tranquil: “...”

The atmosphere turned awkward.

In the void, even the Heavenly Emperor’s daughter couldn’t bear to watch.

The awkward atmosphere made her uneasy.

Therefore, she made her move.

“Future Sword – Live as long as the universe, shine as the sun and moon!” The Heavenly Emperor swept her sword across.

This sword, passing through ‘the present’, appeared right beside Golden Tranquil.

And coincidentally, Golden Tranquil instinctively dodged to the left.

Her evasion led her right into the path of the Heavenly Emperor’s sword light.

The sword light shaved off, removing the golden coating on Golden Tranquil’s skin, revealing an inner body as beautiful as glass gemstones.

Chapter 2970: Chapter 2968: Perfect Saber Intent Armor
The effect of the Heavenly Emperor’s Son’s “Future Sword” seems to have the ‘Guaranteed Hit’ effect, similar to the Ancient Nether Clone’s spear technique ‘Karmic Spear’ in the Black Dragon World.

However, the ‘Karmic Spear’ is a method of reversing karmic causality.

And the “Future Sword” doesn’t strike the present—it strikes the future!

The moment the sword is swung, under the influence of temporal laws, the target is bound to be hit by this strike unless you can master a method to counteract the ‘Space-Time Traversal’.

Golden Tranquil dodged the ‘present’ but then collided with the sword light of the “Future Sword.” A layer of golden paint was scraped off, revealing the interior beneath the coat of gold.

Song Shuhang, who had been observing Golden Tranquil with the ‘Heavenly Dao’s Vision,’ slightly focused his gaze, locking onto the scraped area of Golden Tranquil.

The body beneath, clear and pretty like glass gemstones, seemed very familiar.

“So that’s it, it’s just a layer of golden paint,” Song Shuhang slowly said.

In all the myriad practitioners in the universe, the only one who would do this, and to oneself no less, is probably just one.

“Repainting is expensive,” Golden Tranquil said nonchalantly after being hit by a sword from the Heavenly Emperor’s Son—perhaps because her face also had a layer of golden paint, her true complexion couldn’t be seen.

From the outside, apart from having a layer of paint scraped off, her main body seemed to be unharmed.

It must be noted that the Heavenly Emperor’s Son’s recent sword strike was not a mere probing cut but a real sword technique imbued with killing intent.

“Fellow friend, someone is trying to chop you down, and you’re worried about some paint?” the Bone Dragon Artifact Spirit couldn’t help but say.

It’s like someone across from you is coming at you with a knife, and you’re concerned about a tear in your clothes?

Focus on what’s important!

Your life is at risk, and yet you’re worried about some paint?

“Don’t underestimate this gold paint. Although it’s just a scratch on the surface, if I want to fix it, I have to repaint this whole area. And the color tone of the repainted area won’t match the original, making it impossible to restore perfectly,” Golden Tranquil pointed at the region on her shoulder as she spoke.

Bone Dragon Artifact Spirit: “...”

“By the way, Artifact Spirit fellow friend, would you like some paint? Aside from Domineering Gold and Stylish Silver, I’ve also developed Noble Purple, Melancholy Blue, and Vibrant Multicolor. There’s definitely one that would suit you!” Golden Tranquil took the opportunity to pitch her products.

“...” Bone Dragon Artifact Spirit: “Fellow friend, you should focus on saving your own life first.”

“No worries, I don’t actually have any major conflict with the Heavenly Emperor’s Son. If I let her chop at me a few times, she’ll calm down,” Golden Tranquil waved her hand nonchalantly.

Bone Dragon Artifact Spirit: “...”

Song Shuhang: “...”

“Hehe.” A pleasant...sneer echoed from the void.

Some people’s voice lines just aren’t meant for sneering. Even the coldest laugh from them doesn’t sound threatening—in this case, Soft Feather’s voice line was such, not suited for a cold demeanor.

A few sword strikes to cool off?

Simply wishful thinking.

The relationship between her, Cheng Lin, and Song Shuhang qualifies as a life-or-death struggle.

Song Shuhang and Cheng Lin want her.

She equally yearns for Song Shuhang and Cheng Lin.

Neither side will give in.

“Since you want to stand there and let me land a few strikes to vent, then just stand still,” said the Heavenly Emperor’s Son Ping, raising her sword in hand.

The weight of many years bore down on the tip of the sword.

Powerful enough to ‘Destroy Stars,’ those laws and power were concentrated at the tip of the Heavenly Emperor’s Son’s sword.

If this strike were to land, even if the power was controlled and compressed, neither the mysterious island nor the dragon tomb would survive the aftermath.

“Don’t fight here! Please, don’t fight in this place!” the Fairy with silver hair and a scar on her back couldn’t help but stand up and plead.

She didn’t want her shelter to be destroyed.

“No need to worry,” the Heavenly Emperor’s Son fluttered the long sword in hand, and the power that was previously concentrated at the tip of the sword was further compressed to a tiny pinpoint: “The moment I kill him, I’ll instantly teleport away.”

This degree of control was something the Heavenly Emperor’s Son could still achieve.

“Don’t move a muscle, just stand there, Cheng Lin,” ordered the Heavenly Emperor’s son as he thrust his sword forward.

“You’ve got the wrong person... Fairy,” the golden-hued Cheng Lin’s figure turned into nothingness, vanishing beside the dragon tomb.

There are only two kinds of people who would not dodge such a strike.

One is truly badass.

The other is truly foolish.

And she was neither.

“Actually, my name is Cheng Goudan. Cheng Lin is really dead, truly dead... You don’t believe it? Why don’t you divinate it?” At the same time as she turned into nothingness, the lingering voice of golden Cheng Lin called out.

“Whether you’re Cheng Goudan, Golden Goudan, or Silver Goudan, the outcome will be the same,” the Heavenly Emperor’s son said as he flicked his arm, creating a flourish of his sword in the vacuum!

She hadn’t been standing still in the vacuum, refraining from acting just to watch the show.

The space near the mysterious island was already under the absolute spatial sealing array she had laid out.

Around the edges of the dragon tomb, she had secretly scattered many new kinds of Spatial Imprisonment Techniques.

Her Spatial Imprisonment Techniques weren’t just simple spatial locks... they were true ‘Space-Time Imprisonments.’

The powers of both time and space here transformed into the ‘domain’ of the Heavenly Emperor’s son.

The once nothingness-transformed golden Cheng Lin was suddenly forced out of her ‘void’ state.

Then, just like the ‘Future Sword,’ countless beams of sword light burst forth in the vacuum, relentlessly striking the golden Cheng Lin.

Each beam of sword light stripped away a piece of golden paint from her body.

The clouds of golden paint turned to powder and drifted down from the sky...

A small part of it fell into a groove of the crystal coffin, mixing with the fresh blood that golden Cheng Lin had previously placed there.

On the crystal coffin, the formation that The White Dragon had set up by herself lit up faintly once more.

Neither the confronting golden Cheng Lin nor the Heavenly Emperor’s son noticed this subtle change.

However, Song Shuhang, who was observing the world meticulously through the ‘Heavenly Dao’s Vision’ mode, keenly caught onto it.

‘Golden paint powder + fresh blood’?

Or maybe, The White Dragon didn’t need fresh blood to resurrect... but instead, the gold paint?

Could the pattern on the crystal coffin be a setup to collect gold paint for her?

Even in resurrection, she wanted to come back in the form of the ‘ancestral golden dragon’?

[Should I privately message The White Dragon and ask for the answer?]

The thought flashed by and was temporarily stored in his ‘memo’ in memory.

Then, Song Shuhang’s gaze once again locked onto Cheng Lin.

At this moment, Cheng Lin, stripped of all her golden paint, revealed her complete, shiny, glass-like body, glistening like a piece of art.

Cheng Lin sighed softly as she circulated her true qi.

In the next moment, a set of exquisite ‘female armor’ covered her body, arming her.

Armor intent?!

No, it was saber intent!

The full name: saber intent armor.

Before Tyrannical Song, it seemed no one among the myriad practitioners in the universe had ever managed to develop this special type of saber intent.

But now, it materialized and took shape on ‘glassy Cheng Lin.’

The exquisite saber intent armor fitted glassy Cheng Lin’s figure perfectly, except for the crooked daoist cap on her head. Everywhere else, the saber intent armor was flawless.

Song Shuhang, perceiving through Heavenly Dao’s View, let out a soft sigh, and then he focused his mind, staring intently at glassy Cheng Lin.

He wanted to try whether Heavenly Dao’s Vision had the ability to appraise or check an item’s attributes.

Chapter 2971: Chapter 2969: Ding~ Homeless Little Song Song added you as a friend
Song Shuhang had confirmed from the very beginning that this Cheng Lin, originally golden and now of a glass gemstone color, was not the “Cheng Goudan” he had been in contact with.

He was clear on this point.

However, from many characteristics, although the glass gemstone-colored Cheng Lin was not the “Cheng Goudan” Song Shuhang knew, she might indeed be the real Cheng Lin.

This point is actually not hard to understand—because as a fragment of “Ghost God Cheng Lin,” Cheng Goudan can fuse with other fragments.

Father Goudan had also assigned Song Shuhang a long-term task of ‘collecting Cheng Lin’s fragments.’

Unfortunately, Song Shuhang cultivated until he reached the Immortal Realm and hadn’t encountered any other fragments of Cheng Lin.

And now, the true identity of this glass gemstone-colored Cheng Lin, if not mistaken, should be Song Shuhang.

Apart from Song Shuhang, no one else would be so unreserved to come before The White Dragon’s dragon tomb with such a confident expression, intending to resurrect her using blood.

Added to that are his peculiar fancy for applying golden paint...and that glass-like body, along with many details.

It is evident that the glass gemstone-colored Cheng Lin•Song Shuhang never intended to hide his real identity from the very beginning.

Song Shuhang guessed that the other party was Song Shuhang.

But what he wanted to ‘see’ clearly was the deeper identity of Song Shuhang—the culprit who led to him being mistaken and severely beaten by The White Dragon, Heavenly Bamboo Shoot, and leaders from the ancient Heavenly City—his true identity!

In fact, quite early on, Song Shuhang had speculated about the identity of ‘Song Shuhang.’

But he had no evidence, and it was just a speculation.

Moreover, with too many karmic entanglements on Song Shuhang, Song Shuhang hadn’t shared his thoughts with anyone.

Now, with the help of Heavenly Dao’s Vision, he just might validate his thoughts.

As a thought arose in Song Shuhang, Daoist Senior lent him the ‘Heavenly Dao’s Vision,’ which truly materialized the corresponding function.

A row of ‘profile’ information emerged beside the glass gemstone-colored Cheng Lin.

[Two-fifths Ghost God•Cheng Lin•Tyrannical Saber Song One]

[Major Event•Tyrannical Saber Song One: Ancient Heavenly City member ‘Song Shuhang,’ a renowned member during the Heavenly City era. In the later stages of the ancient Heavenly City, he stole the ‘Heavenly Emperor’s Mandate,’ and at the end of the ancient Heavenly City era, he replaced the ‘Heavenly Emperor’ in power, attempting to obliterate the ‘Ancient Heavenly City’s path’ from within...The obliteration of Heavenly City’s path failed; Plan A failed, Dao shattered and collapsed.]

[Major Event•Cheng Lin: ‘Jade Lake Empress’ from the ancient Heavenly City, a top-tier immortal among the Heavenly City era, ranked alongside the Four Great Emperors and the Ancestral Dragon. After the failure of Plan A, she took the lead in directing Plan B, inheriting the collapsed Tyrannical Saber Song One, the destroyer of the Heavenly City.]

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

He initially wanted to see if he could find the answers he sought from ‘Song Shuhang.’

But instead, he unearthed major news.

In the middle and later stages of the ancient Heavenly City era, Song Shuhang had already stolen the Heavenly Emperor’s mandate?

And, at the end of the Heavenly City era, he even replaced the Heavenly Emperor’s child to become the Heavenly Emperor?

Did the people of the Heavenly City not notice that the ‘Heavenly Emperor’ had been switched out?

Da Da Zi, this Heavenly Emperor, was he a bit wronged?

And how did he manage it? Secretly replacing the Heavenly Emperor’s child?

[Let’s note this down in the memo first, and go directly to ask the persons involved, Cheng Goudan and Da Da Zi, later.]

Song Shuhang noted it down first.

He then continued to focus on the glass gemstone Cheng Lin, reading deeper layers of information.

Beneath, the glass gemstone Cheng Lin, wearing ‘saber intent armor,’ suddenly shivered.

“Really, Song Shuhang sometimes is just too impatient.” She whispered, “At least, let me clear the obstacles for you before I die...make full use of me, don’t let me die in vain.”

As she spoke, she gestured in the vacuum, projecting a ‘QR code.’

It was the QR code for adding someone to the ‘Cultivator Chat System.’

Cheng Lin had always preserved this “QR code.”

In the void.

When the Heavenly Emperor’s Son saw Cheng Lin suddenly produce this pattern, he frowned and paused his attack.

Below.

Seeing that the Heavenly Emperor’s Son paused his attack, glass gemstones Cheng Lin turned back and resumed her operations.

She gently swept her mental energy over this “QR code.”

[Ding~ Congratulations, you have added ‘Big Shot Tyrannical Song’ as a friend. From now on, there is no distance between you, regardless of the ends of the world, no matter how far, both hearts can communicate without any barriers.]

Song Shuhang, on his part, also received the notification of a new friend request at the same time.

[Ding~ New user ‘Song Shuhang’ requests to add you as a friend—do you agree? Choose yes!]

[Automatic title generation in progress...]

[Homeless Little Song Song]

[Your new friend and [Blacklist 1•Dead Fairy Cheng Goudan], [Crisp (Crossed Out) Beautiful Forehead] Slow-Witted Song, [Orthopedics Department] Immortal Fairy White Bones, [Golden Dragon Scarf] The White Dragon, [Heavens] Senior Turtle... might know each other. Would you like to add them to [Nine Provinces Number Two Group] or [Da Dazi’s Heavenly Court] group?]

The ‘Cultivator Chat System’ proactively recommended this to Song Shuhang—it was clearly a new function churned out on overtime by Lady Kunna, making the ‘Cultivator Chat’ more user-friendly.

Something stirred in Song Shuhang’s mind.

He reached out to add the new member to the ‘Nine Provinces Number Two Group.’

Since it was the server itself adding a person, all members of Group Two received a ‘system alert’ as soon as he joined.

[Homeless Little Song Song] Song Wood: “!!!”

Private chat, huh? Why add me to the group?

Yo, Dragon Sister, I’m at the Mysterious Island Dragon Tomb. What are your conditions for revival? Song Wood quickly texted.

Chapter 2972: Chapter 2970: The Influence of the Will of the Heavens
Even Song Shuhang, who had been seasoned through the trials of the Nine Provinces Number One Group, was momentarily stunned.

However, it only lasted for less than an instant.

Sometimes, you just got to brush off the nonsense talk; take it seriously and you lose.

But...

Could something like time travel truly be achieved?

Song Shuhang’s own “dreamland” skill could let him dream of the past, but after all, the dreamland was just an illusion, like accessing a memory and personally experiencing it.

The reason “dreamland” could affect the past was related to the strength of the one being dreamt of.

Only those whose strength surpassed beings like Senior Scarlet Heaven could sense Song Shuhang in his dreamland state—this sensing was based on the great ones’ powerful intuition, as well as methods like divinations of the “future”.

If the subject of the dreamland could not sense Song Shuhang, then he couldn’t possibly cause the slightest impact on the “past”.

“Can something like time travel really be done?” Song Shuhang suddenly inquired.

On the other side, Little Song Song, the one without a home: “...”

No techniques work against the non-technique; Song Shuhang didn’t respond to his nonsense talk. Even if his verbal attack skills were maxed out, they were ineffective. Without serious conversation, Song Shuhang might end up talked to death.

“Normally, it’s impossible. Any entity with physical substance thinking of time travel... the rules of the Heavenly Dao would certainly not permit such a thing to happen,” Little Song Song without a home said after a moment’s thought. “Unless, it’s like the ‘dreamland state’ your dad has.”

Song Shuhang reflected on this.

Besides his own ‘dreamland,’ he also remembered the ‘Future Child’ form of Soft Feather.

He had encountered that special state of Soft Feather.

“Then, what’s your story?” Song Shuhang asked.

Little Song Song without a home: “Dad, you’re asking this in a very professional way... My answer is, I know nothing.”

That was the truth; he did not have an answer himself either.

Song Shuhang: “...”

Was the person opposite to him now addicted to acting? Calling him dad always felt like calling his own father.

“I know you, dad, have many questions for me, and after some time... It won’t be long, I will return. By then, everything about me will come back with my return. The answers you seek will all be answered,” Little Song Song without a home continued.

With this, he made his identity official.

—The vanished petty ghost spirit would return soon, possibly bringing back all its memories and... power?

Song Shuhang raised his eyebrows slightly as he read this reply.

He had thought his heart would be complicated when he got this answer.

But to his surprise, when he actually heard the reply, Song Shuhang found his heart to be undisturbed!

He had a great heart passed down from his ancestors, and his mind and willpower were fairly firm, he had experienced much.

But such tranquility at this moment was clearly abnormal.

It seemed that there was nothing left in the world that could still surprise him.

“This state is clearly not right,” Song Shuhang furrowed his brows.

After a bit of thought, he guessed a possibility.

Could it be the influence of the Heavenly Dao’s vision?

The Heavenly Dao, the information of eternity, combined with the ‘Heavenly Dao’s View’ Daozi shared with him, these things might be affecting him continuously.

Once the cumulative effect reached a certain level, Song Shuhang’s heart would become ‘undisturbed’.

In the face of any information from the myriad practitioners in the universe, he could not stir any emotion.

“Is it that each Heavenly Dao is affected? Or is the ‘incomplete’ Heavenly Dao being disturbed by ‘Heaven’s Will’?”

Upon further thought, the fat ball, which was the Heavenly Dao, seemed to have entered robot mode in the later stages, mechanically enforcing the laws of the Heavenly Dao and processing events programmatically.

Could it be that the flight of each Heavenly Dao is related to this issue as well?

After a calm contemplation, Song Shuhang noted this down in his ‘memorandum’ to discuss thoroughly with Senior White, Senior White two, Father Goudan, and the three-eyed young senior once the ‘dreamland’ ended.

Then, Song Shuhang replied, “Do you have something else to do? Why do you need to wait a while before returning? Is my current state still unable to withstand it?”

After all, Song Shuhang had already stepped onto the Path of Seeking Life Through Death and had become a true Immortal.

If not even an ‘Immortal’ could withstand it, did he need to aim for pseudo-immortality?

“Now, I have completed the ancient Heavenly City’s obsession with the help of Daozi’s hand. However, there are some things that I would like to settle at the end.” Little Song Song without a home replied—and moreover, if Daozi completes the mission of the 8.5th Heavenly Dao and enters the official 9th Heavenly Dao battle, he would need to use the ceremonial formation to extract and resurrect the ‘portion of existence’ that Daozi had previously preserved.

Song Shuhang: “Alright.”

To be honest...

Song Shuhang’s strength was already to the point where he was indifferent to one more or one less pendant.

The pendants on him were all incredibly powerful, basically starting from Immortal or divine weapons, one more wouldn’t matter, one less wouldn’t hurt.

Therefore, whether petty ghost spirit number one chose to return now or later wasn’t urgent for Song Shuhang; he was just casually inquiring.

By contrast, it was a big question how to handle the personal relationships when the other party returned.

“Also... if you, dad, are using ‘Heavenly Dao’s View’ to watch the myriad realms, you should have seen that scene, right?” Little Song Song without a home suddenly brought up.

“The Stellar Destruction Virus?” Song Shuhang asked.

Little Song Song without a home: “Yes.”

“Daozi’s consciousness has returned... He should be about to take action against these ‘Stellar Destruction Viruses’,” Song Shuhang said aloud.

As he spoke, Daozi’s intent resurfaced, pressing down on the myriad practitioners in the universe.

“Sorry to keep you waiting, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song,” Daozi spoke.

He had just taken a moment to rest, to recover, and to familiarize himself with the ‘Heaven’s Will’.

“Not at all—I have gained many insights into the myriad realms through ‘Heavenly Dao’s Vision,’ and I have yet to thank Daozi for it,” Song Shuhang replied.

“That’s good then,” Daozi emitted an emotionless chuckle.

Though laughing, the laugh was without a ripple.

He seemed to have been affected by the information of eternity as well.

“If Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song is ready, then experience my actions carefully next. It might be helpful for you to condense your second path to immortality,” Daozi added.

He was only affected, but his reason and thoughts were not problematic.

Song Shuhang nodded without saying anything further, and calmly maintained the link with Daozi through the ‘dreamland’.

What followed was Daozi’s time to enforce the laws.

Chapter 2973: Chapter 2971: Then kill the person who’s pressing the nuclear button!
“`

Under Song Shuhang’s sensing, Daozi reached out and started to act within the vacuum.

The principles belonging to the Heavenly Dao were being pulled over one by one.

—To Song Shuhang, this process seemed like it was “pixelated,” unclear to see.

In the myriad practitioners in the universe, every star that had been infected with the “virus” felt the pull of the laws of the Heavenly Dao.

Daozi wanted to use the “Heavenly Dao Authority” to directly eradicate the viruses from the stars of the myriad practitioners in the universe, completely destroying all the viruses.

[Will it be successful?] Song Shuhang looked forward to the scenes of the myriad practitioners in the universe with some anticipation.

But at this time, his heart remained eerily calm.

Even at the moment “Daozi” made his move, Song Shuhang had already faintly sensed the outcome of Daozi’s action deep in his heart!

Whoosh~

First, across the myriad realms plane, a large portion of “stars” had their replicating “viruses” pulled out!

These viruses were categories of the “Stellar Destruction Virus” that kept on spreading.

Children and grandchildren, endless generations of viruses... They differed greatly from the Virus Mother Body.

These “great-great-grandchildren” viruses could not resist the lure of the Heavenly Dao Authority and were uprooted.

With Daozi’s command of “Annihilation,” these viruses instantly turned to ashes!

Song Shuhang carefully experienced the details of Daozi’s actions, and his comprehension of the Will of the Heavens related to the “Cultivator Chat System” suddenly deepened a bit more.

This time, what deepened was the comprehension related to “authority and commands.”

Whether it was seeing through the Heavenly Dao or attaching to it to sense its use of authority, both could enhance Song Shuhang’s comprehension of the Will of the Heavens related to the “Cultivator Chat System”—this second Will of the Heavens seemed to be aiming to comprehend all the functions of the “Heavenly Dao.”

Next is the region with the “Void Sun Guardians” clones staying in some of the stars.

In these regions, the Void Sun Guardian clones are obtaining “undying components” through some means and constantly creating “Stellar Destruction Viruses” with them.

Under the compulsion of the “Daozi” Heavenly Dao Authority, even the clones of the Void Sun Guardians couldn’t keep all the “Stellar Destruction Viruses.”

These viruses, too, were forcibly extracted by the Heavenly Dao Authority and began to enter the annihilation phase.

But obviously, these viruses, which were made with similar “undying components” to Cloud Gauze Three View Moon or Tyrannical Song, were more difficult to handle.

They were permeated with the “aura of eternity,” and when faced with the Heavenly Dao Authority’s effort to deal with them, they could even resist for a short time!

Using eternity to combat eternity.

As for the clones of the “Void Sun Guardians,” upon sensing the coercive measures of the Will of the Heavens, they instantly began to withdraw. Some of the “Void Sun Guardian clones” even dissolved on the spot, dissipating without a trace.

The existence of the Immortal Realm is still nothing to the “Heavenly Dao”... but for “Daozi,” who could only count as ‘half a Heavenly Dao,’ eradicating them root and branch would take some effort.

And Daozi was currently focusing all his effort on the “viruses.”

The converging and fleeing “Void Sun Guardians” would have to be given a chance to catch their breath for now.

...

...

About ten breaths’ time had passed since Daozi made his move... and at least seventy percent of the infected “stars” were rescued!

During this period, Song Shuhang saw that inside these “stars,” there were forces of the virtuous network hidden.

—The legacy of Daoist Priest Virtue to suppress the “Stellar Destruction Virus” was secretly assisting “Daozi’s” actions, working with him to uproot the viral menace.

This was also why “Daozi’s” actions were so smooth.

Even those viruses made with “undying components” were actually being suppressed by the virtuous network!

A few moments later...

The majority of the viruses made with “undying components” were wiped out, and finally, a batch of special “Constant Star Destruction Virus Mother Bodies” appeared before “Daozi” and Song Shuhang.

These “Virus Mother Bodies” were guarded by both the Void Sun Guardians and the Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls.

“`

“Annihilate!” Daozi issued the annihilation command without hesitation.

—He had just managed to help Confucianism through a crisis, allowing the resurrection of the Confucian junior brothers and sisters to no longer be incomplete, providing a chance for the Confucian system to thrive once again.

But now, someone was actually fiddling with the idea of destroying the world.

Daozi certainly wouldn’t be courteous.

Today, he intended to completely cleanse the “virus.”

Boom~

The “laws of the Heavenly Dao” activated by Daozi acted upon the star, directly pulling at that portion of the “Stellar Destruction Virus Mother Body.”

The clones of the Void Sun Guardians and the Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls by his side couldn’t withstand it, their bodies were blown away, and cracks appeared all over them.

These cracks couldn’t be healed with ordinary self-recovery methods, after all, they bore the marks left by the Will of the Heavens.

The Stellar Destruction Virus Mother Body was washed layer by layer by the “laws of the Heavenly Dao.”

The virus’s outer shell was completely eroded away... revealing its core at last.

It was an object that looked like a grain of iron.

“It’s indeed meticulous to say that iron is the star’s doomsday,” Song Shuhang thought to himself with a strange calmness.

While contemplating, the annihilation power of the Heavenly Dao washed over the iron grain-like object.

But at that moment, an “immortal” aura emerged from those tiny iron grains...

Just like Song Shuhang’s “undying fat whale golden core” or Cloud Gauze Three View Moon’s “bone of eternity.”

Both possessed eternal energy but lacked the authority of the Heavenly Dao—an Immortal Material!

Eternity was an attribute that even the authority of the Heavenly Dao couldn’t breach... Once, there was a Daozi who couldn’t even change his hairstyle at will.

The moment one becomes “immortal,” even the state of one’s body and nails at that instant would be fixed in eternity.

Not even the Heavenly Dao could cut its own hair.

At this moment, Daozi’s “Annihilation Command” also failed to completely obliterate these “iron grain materials.”

“It really is so...” Song Shuhang whispered inwardly.

In fact, Daozi wasn’t the first Heavenly Dao to do such a thing; Immortal Daoist Virtue had also done similar acts against the Stellar Destruction Virus before.

The virus offspring born and spread from the Virus Mother Body could be destroyed by the authority of the Heavenly Dao.

But this Mother Body, with its eternal attributes, remained untouchable even by the authority of the Heavenly Dao!

“Immortal?” Daozi spoke calmly, yet even in his calm tone, one could sense a hint of surprise from Senior Daozi.

“Yes... indestructible and eternal,” Song Shuhang spoke up.

Daozi furrowed his brows, his fingers tapping on the Throne of Wealth’s armrest.

Using something indestructible and eternal as the “virus” mother body...

Not even the authority of the Heavenly Dao could erase them.

What to do now?

“Is it only possible to let them be? Or should they be sealed?” Daozi was somewhat unwilling.

“Perhaps, I have a way,” Song Shuhang said.

These virus mother bodies were indeed terrifying; they were like atomic bombs, highly threatening once detonated.

However, since the “virus mother bodies” couldn’t be dealt with, could the mastermind controlling them be dealt with instead?

If you can’t bomb the atomic bomb, then take out the person holding the button for it.

With a thought, Song Shuhang began to summon his “Cultivator Chat System.”

The “restorable gray account” he held in his hand was about to be put to use!

Chapter 2974: Chapter 2972: Haha, this wave is stable!
In the myriad realms, the big players always have a variety of clever maneuvers.

And the big player hidden behind the ‘Void Sun Guardians’ and ‘Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls’ had means that were particularly cunning.

It had quietly downloaded the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ client and even registered an account...

But its intention in registering was not to use the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ normally but to study and hack it. It attempted to seize control of the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ when Song Shuhang exploded into a bloody mist, aiming to turn the tables.

Regrettably, it miscalculated the primary and secondary relationship between the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ and Song Shuhang and also underestimated the system’s uniqueness.

The big player’s plan to seize control of the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ failed.

At the moment of failure, it immediately used its clever maneuvers to erase its account, deleting the account and exiting!

If it wasn’t for Song Shuhang’s ‘undying fat whale golden core’ also quietly restoring the ‘data’ during its resurrection, maybe this big player behind the scenes would have succeeded.

Now, Song Shuhang held a restored ‘grey offline ID account’ in his hands.

This account was closely linked to the big player behind the scenes.

As long as he used it, Song Shuhang could lock onto the other party’s location and track them down.

If the problem can’t be solved... then let’s solve the person who caused this problem!

Song Shuhang shared his thoughts with Daozi.

[Directly dealing with the existence that created the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’? If it’s feasible, that would indeed be a good idea,] Daozi pondered and replied.

However, to go through with this, a preventative measure would be necessary for the myriad realms.

–If the person pulling the strings behind the scenes could be killed by him, there would be two possible outcomes.

One is that this crisis would be averted, which would be cause for celebration.

The second is that upon the death of the string-puller, all the Stellar Destruction Viruses might go out of control and trigger instant self-destruction, dragging down a large swath of the myriad realms with it. This would have to be guarded against.

–But it’s also possible that the figure behind it all won’t be so easily dealt with.

After all, they hold the true ‘immortal information’ and might themselves be in an immortal state.

In that case, going directly to their doorstep could not only fail to resolve the issue but also trigger their deeper vigilance, losing the element of surprise afforded by Song Shuhang’s ‘grey ID account’.

This too had to be guarded against.

[I need to make some preparations,] Daozi said to Song Shuhang, [Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, your state is about to end, so be ready to ‘Exit Dream’ at any moment. Then, in the final moments of your state, I will try my best to conceal your actions. Let’s hope that when you use the ‘grey ID account’ to lock onto the other party, they won’t detect it...]

[Alright,] Song Shuhang nodded in response.

Daozi once again sought to buy time, easing the state he was in.

At the same time, he began trying to communicate with that ‘Virtuous Network’ in all the myriad realms—when Song Shuhang was using ‘Heavenly Dao’s Vision’ to observe the myriad realms, Daozi also shared the details Song Shuhang was focusing on.

He had seen how this virtuous network had assisted him while he was dealing with the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’.

This formidable virtuous network was a creation of the Heavenly Dao!

It was probably left behind by one of the previous Wielders of the Will during their tenure.

The purpose of the virtuous network was clear, to counter the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’ and to suppress it.

If he could borrow the power of this virtuous network, he could patch up his next action—if killing the ‘person pulling the strings’ led to an uncontrollable outbreak of the virus, the virtuous network could suppress the viruses.

Afterward, Daozi could free up his hands to either seal these viruses or slowly deal with them.

A moment later...

Daozi successfully connected with the virtuous network, which upon sensing that Daozi’s target was the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’, agreed immediately to his access request.

[Good, now we have our preventative measure,] Daozi thought to himself.

Taking advantage of the last moments, Daozi began using the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ to strengthen the ‘Virtuous Network’, striving to boost it to its peak condition.

“`

Daozi’s actions directly benefited ‘Sage Monarch Melon Eater,’ who was overcoming tribulation.

The reinforcement of the virtuous network allowed Sage Monarch Melon Eater to soar in the sea of heavenly tribulation as if a whale had grown wings!

...

...

About twenty breaths later.

“Are you ready, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song?” Daozi asked.

“All set,” Song Shuhang replied.

Daozi said in a deep voice, “Next, I will conceal your actions, and you will lock onto the opponent.”

The Will of the Heavens took action personally, stirring up all heaven’s secrets related to Song Shuhang.

They strived to prevent the opponent from detecting Song Shuhang’s actions and to preserve the effects of this ‘Grey ID Account’ as much as possible.

In case... if he could not deal with the opponent, they might have to rely on the ‘Grey ID Account’ again in the future to lock onto the opponent and deal with this person behind the scenes.

Daozi did not have blind confidence in his Heavenly Dao Authority; he had left himself a way out.

In case he wasn’t up to the task, there were still Tyrannical Song and Fellow Daoist White or others who could step in.

After stirring up Song Shuhang’s heaven’s secrets, Daozi thought for a moment and decided to further enhance the concealing effect.

He simply veiled all the ‘Heavenly Mechanism’ of the entire myriad practitioners in the universe.

Heavenly Mechanism became obscured; at this moment, all divination methods in the myriad practitioners in the universe lost their effect.

Even the ‘intuition’ of crisis for the big shots was blocked.

This was Daozi’s double protection for Song Shuhang.

If only Song Shuhang was shielded, it would be like a sign proclaiming ‘No Silver Here,’ and the opponent, upon divination, could easily guess the reason upon finding only Song Shuhang’s heavenly secrets were concealed.

But by shielding the heavenly secrets of the entire myriad practitioners in the universe, the opponent would be unable to figure out anything—under such circumstances, the secondary shielding on Song Shuhang would achieve a perfect effect.

All cultivators in the myriad practitioners in the universe felt a stir in their hearts at this moment.

“Here it comes again, that feeling of heart movement,” the Almighty Merchant said slowly as he looked up at the sky—he too had a connection with the ‘Virtuous Network.’

With the heavenly secrets of the entire myriad practitioners in the universe concealed, what major action is the Will of the Heavens planning now?

Elsewhere.

The ‘Void Sun Guardians’ and ‘Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull’ from the myriad practitioners in the universe also began to grow uneasy.

If you really stir up a big incident, you might even be struck down along the internet cables.

It’s now in Senior White’s territory.

Ha, this round is secure!

Chapter 2975: Chapter 2973: It’s actually you, Ball Sky Path!
Perhaps sometimes, the most dangerous place is actually the safest — under the principle of “darkness beneath the light.”

However, when facing Senior White, this principle is certainly inapplicable.

If one is related to Senior White, and moreover stands in opposition to him... then the most dangerous place truly becomes the most perilous, devoid of any sense of security.

“It’s the Dream Realm, hidden right here,” Song Shuhang conveyed the clue to Daozi.

At the same time, a thought emerged in his heart.

Previously, Senior White was in a hurry to perfect the ‘God Creation Plan,’ forming the ‘World Tree’ in the Dream Realm and taking control of the Dream Realm’s sector lord authority... could it be because Senior White was instinctively preparing for this scenario?

At the end of last year, it was the only time since Song Shuhang had met Senior White that he noticed Senior White urgently wanted to accomplish something.

At that time, Senior White’s pace of life suddenly became hurried, as if summer vacation was about to end and homework was due soon.

It must be right!

The urgency of Senior White’s ‘God Creation Plan,’ with the timing set just before this critical moment, must mean that Senior White was instinctively preparing for this event and incidentally suppressing the entity pulling the strings.

Perhaps when ‘Daozi’ directly confronts the mastermind later, Senior White’s arrangements in the Dream Realm could also come into play!

This wave is steady —

This is Senior White’s home ground, and he stands on his side. There’s no reason to lose!

[“Go on, Senior Daozi!”] Song Shuhang was brimming with boldness, as though he had already seen victory.

Daozi’s demeanor, influenced by the ‘Heavenly Will’ and thus calmed, seemed at this moment to be affected by Song Shuhang’s spirit, stirring a sense of valor.

[“Let’s see who you really are,”] Daozi said solemnly.

In the state where the Heavenly Dao blocks the Heavenly Mechanism of the Myriad Realms, even one’s ‘Crisis Intuition’ can be affected.

Daozi exercised the Heavenly Dao Authority, and the intent of the Heavenly Dao descended directly to a coordinate in the Dream Realm.

That location was a connected area between the Dream Realm and the ‘Chaos Heavenly World.’

The Chaos Heavenly World is one of the myriad realms’ planes and is a rare world still retaining many ancient ruins from ancient times.

And that mastermind behind the scenes was, at this moment, residing within an interspatial pocket where the Dream Realm and the Chaos Heavenly World intersect.

The interspatial pocket belongs to the range of the Dream Realm, with a separate world within.

Daozi’s ‘Will of the Heavenly Dao’ broke directly into this pocket.

“Dissipate,” the intent of Daozi commanded.

As soon as these words were spoken, the barrier simulating the effects of the ‘small black room’ was directly erased.

At the same time, the camouflaged mastermind hidden in the interspatial layer also became aware of Daozi’s arrival — in fact, as soon as Daozi began to eliminate the stellar viruses in the myriad practitioners in the universe, the mastermind was already prepared.

It just didn’t expect Daozi to find it so quickly!

Daozi’s intent entered this ‘interspatial world,’ surveying the surroundings — his intent was the vanguard, and at the same time, Daozi’s ‘Body of Eternity’ was also ready, prepared to step into the main world at any moment.

The vision of Song Shuhang’s dreamland skill attached itself to Daozi’s intent, allowing him to see the interspatial world.

It was a world akin to a desert.

In this world, aside from small mounds of earth scattered about, there was nothing else.

Upon closer inspection, it could be seen that those black mounds were actually comprised of particles resembling ‘Black Iron Sand,’ piled up on top of one another.

Daozi’s intent focused his gaze.

Each and every one of those small mounds of dark earth were composed of ‘pseudo-eternal parts’.

At the core of each little mound, there was a grain of genuine ‘Immortal Iron Sand’—objects that carry the aura of eternity, which not even the Heavenly Dao Authority could erase.

Daozi’s gaze finally settled on the center of the interspatial pocket.

It was the target that Song Shuhang and Daozi were searching for.

The Dark Sun appeared insubstantial, more like an illusion—an entity with a state similar to the ‘Void Sun Guardians’ outside.

When confronted with Daozi’s unyielding intent, the Dark Sun on the opposite side showed no signs of fear.

It calmly ‘gazed’ back at Daozi’s intent, standing opposite Daozi with an attitude of equality.

Daozi’s intent let out a silent sigh—indeed, the other party possessed an ‘eternity’ that Daozi least wanted to encounter.

[Apart from the aura of eternity... it bears the scent of the ‘ruler of the Netherworld.’] Song Shuhang, who was delving into the dreamland skill, noticed this fact.

The Dark Sun bore a scent belonging to the Netherworld’s ruler.

A scent too familiar to Song Shuhang.

After all, he might be the creature with the best relationship to the ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ throughout ancient and modern times among the myriad practitioners in the universe. He was also the man who had come into contact with the ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ the most.

Even Daozi, the 8.5 Wielder of the Will, did not understand the ruler of the Netherworld as clearly as Song Shuhang did—after all, Daozi hadn’t condensed his own ‘ruler of the Netherworld’.

While Song Shuhang, he had a manifestation, ‘Dark Song.’

Therefore, Song Shuhang detected the presence of the ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ on the other party before ‘Daozi’ did.

[Ruler of the Netherworld? As expected, it involves eternity and also the ruler of the Netherworld... This guy is surely a past incarnation of the Heavenly Way.] Daozi responded.

But which incarnation of the Heavenly Way is the opponent?

[The liquefied metal ball represents the Eighth, above that is Wielder of the Will White, above him is the Immortal Daoist Virtue... and then I’m unclear about the Fifth and Fourth. The Third is Heavenly Dao Goudan’s father, and the Second is Heavenly Dao’s Three Eyes, with no information remaining on the First. If not for Senior Three Eyes being clear about being the Second, maybe even the very concept of a First Heavenly Dao would have been forgotten.] Song Shuhang replied.

Does that mean this Dark Sun Opposite us is either the Fifth or the Fourth Heavenly Dao?

The chance that it is the First Heavenly Dao is very slim since it seems there is no corresponding ‘ruler of the Netherworld.’

But we can’t rule out the contingency plans of other Heavenly Daos—perhaps one of them, like Wielder of the Will White, once severed a part of his Netherworld’s ruler flesh for research, leaving behind this Dark Sun as his backup?

The three-eyed young senior corresponding to the Heavenly Dao’s Three Eyes doesn’t seem to be someone benevolent. The three-eyed young senior is deeply cautious about his own Heavenly Dao.

[One of the Fifth or Fourth Heavenly Daos?] Daozi’s intent calmly faced the other: [I’m about to pull over my fleshly body.]

In face of eternity, he had to bring over his Immortal Body.

Mere ‘intuitive manifestation’ was insufficient to deal with the opponent.

With a thought, the space behind Daozi’s intent waved slightly.

Then, Daozi’s Immortal Body quietly emerged.

An aura of Indestructible settled into the air.

The moment the Heavenly Dao Body appeared, all ‘undying components’ throughout the interspatial pocket scattered!

“You... are not the Ninth Wielder of the Will... Are you Ball Heavenly Dao?” At this moment, the Dark Sun opposite suddenly spoke with a tone of surprise.

Chapter 2976: Chapter 2974: No, you need me! Your body is saying you need me!
Daozi: “???”

Across from him.

This was clearly not the Ninth Heavenly Dao but rather the aura of the Eighth Heavenly Dao “Sphere Heaven Dao,” which had recently ‘collapsed’ before all in the myriad practitioners in the universe!

In other words, this was the backup plan of the Eighth Session Heavenly Dao!

It was Sphere Heaven Dao’s second attempt at proving his Dao!

Was the Sphere Heaven Dao deliberately using ‘collapse’ as a way to exit the Heavenly Dao seat and seek detachment by going through the process of ‘proving his Dao for eternity’ again?

However... it’s easy to talk about a second proving of Dao, but the execution is far from simple.

Among the many sessions of Heavenly Dao so far, only the current ‘Sphere Heaven Dao’ had completed the process of a second proving of Dao.

Nobody knew how he managed it.

Indeed, none who proved their Dao to achieve eternity and became the Heavenly Dao were simple characters!

Even the ‘Daoist Priest Virtue,’ who seemed to have been the weakest link in the history of Heavenly Dao, turned the tables at the last moment. Just as it was about to succeed and truly ‘detach,’ it smashed its plans to smithereens, severing all the karmic ties of myriad practitioners!

Faced with the praise of the Dark Sun, Daozi remained expressionless.

Across from him, the Dark Sun didn’t mind its ‘domain’ being invaded.

But for the Dark Sun, this was good news!

Since the ‘Sphere Heaven Dao’s’ second attempt to detach failed, it meant there was an opportunity for cooperation between it and the ‘Sphere Heaven Dao!’

The Sphere Heaven Dao had failed, so he would need to find a new method for transcendence!

That was the contract for their cooperation!

As long as there was an opportunity for cooperation, the contradiction between the two could be resolved through negotiation.

“So, Sphere Heaven Dao... what you now need is a brand-new, viable Path of Transcendence!” In the midst of the Dark Sun, a black flame sparked, forming a hand extended toward ‘Daozi’: “You need me!”

The Dark Sun, looking at ‘Daozi’.

Chapter 2977: Chapter 2975: Saying No!
Just like ordinary Tribulation Transcenders and Immortals crave for “immortal information,” the true Will of the Heavens similarly possesses an insatiable desire for “Transcendence Information”!

Except for someone like Daoist Priest Virtue, who is a salted fish... That guy is definitely a fake Will of the Heavens.

And since the “Sphere Heavenly Dao” before me has already attempted “transcendence,” a truly viable and flawless “Path of Transcendence” would be an irresistible temptation for it!

The Black Sun believed that the Sphere Heavenly Dao before him would not disappoint.

To offer the entirety of myriad practitioners in the universe as a sacrifice to achieve transcendence.

Chapter 2978: Chapter 2976: Just One Is Enough!
Daozi’s “Immortal Heavenly Dao Body” acted, releasing thousands of threads of power of the Laws from his fingertips. They spread out, pierced the vacuum, infiltrated into the myriad practitioners in the universe, and locked onto all pre-identified targets!

Gather them together for a collective beating.

Past Heavenly Daos who have ‘collapsed’, some have truly dissipated, merged by the ‘laws of the Heavenly Dao.’
