Chapter 2979: Chapter 2977: What are you doing during the New Year, are you free? Can you come to the rescue?

Some things are only interesting because they are unique. Some things, the true power lies in not sharing them with anyone.

“You can’t kill me... Sky Dao. What the nature of ‘eternity’ is, you yourself should know best.” Even though the Dark Sun was shattered time after time, its true nucleus was made of ‘eternal and indestructible’ Heavenly Dao material.

Being shattered and then reassembling was all in a day’s work.

As long as Daozi couldn’t obliterate the ‘eternal and indestructible’ material, it would be impossible to kill it.

——Moreover, unlike the combination of ‘Cloud Gauze Three View Moon + bone of eternity’, the relationship between the Dark Sun and the Indestructible Material originated from the same source, so there was no worry about the ‘Heavenly Dao eternal material’ being seized by others.

Even if the Indestructible Material in its body was forcibly taken away and it exploded, a new entity would still condense atop the Immortal Heavenly Dao Material. Moreover, it could condense upon any grain of ‘Indestructible Material’!

Boom~ Daozi, cold as ice, blasted the Dark Sun apart yet again, continuously weakening the power of the Dark Sun.

The Dark Sun, after all, was no longer the ‘current Heavenly Dao’.

Therefore, theoretically, as long as the battle continued, there would come a moment when its energy would be completely exhausted.

After its energy was entirely depleted, despite its eternal nature, it would have to lie down obediently and no longer cause trouble.

“This is meaningless, Sky Dao. You can’t destroy ‘eternity’ just like you can’t destroy yourself,” said the Dark Sun.

Although it was constantly taking a beating, the Dark Sun retained an unyielding demeanor and never showed weakness with its words.

And it wasn’t truly without the power to counterattack.

Previously, the Dark Sun had also mentioned that the Ninth Heavenly Dao is a very special term of Heavenly Will.

This term of Heavenly Dao... will be a turning point for the world.

This key term of Heavenly Dao, Daozi hopes to have ‘Tyrannical Song’ at the helm.

He trusts Tyrannical Song.

Moreover, there was no one more suitable than Tyrannical Song among those he knew.

In fact, ‘Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven’ was a very suitable candidate for the ‘next Heavenly Will.’ He had the strength, profound knowledge, and a good temperament.

The first time Daozi saw Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven, he even felt that the other’s demeanor was somewhat similar to that of his master ‘Sage of Confucianism.’

Both were very reliable entities.

Unfortunately... Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven did not aspire to be the Heavenly Will; his interest was in nurturing a Heavenly Will to take over.

Beyond Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven, the other acquaintances were either disinterested in the Heavenly Dao or had personality flaws.

[You can do it, Tyrannical Song.]

Internally, Daozi blessed Song Shuhang.

The next term of the Heavenly Dao was too significant, potentially facing the ‘Dark Sun’s’ plan to destroy the world upon taking office.

The responsibility was extremely heavy.

And if by bad luck the Dark Sun broke out early... and the contingencies he left were not of much use, then before the next Heavenly Dao assumed office, it would be starting in hell mode.

I’m afraid that as soon as I take office, I’ll have to face a collapsing myriad practitioners in the universe.

“Not only do I have to beat the time difference, but I also need to give Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song an opportunity for reinforcement. I strive to push him to the position of the Ninth Heavenly Dao in the shortest time possible,” Daozi thought to himself.

Before anyone realized it, Senior White two had become the person in charge of the next action, commanding the overall situation.

Within Song Shuhang’s ‘Tyrant Realm.’

When dreaming through the eyes of the Heavens, observing the myriad practitioners in the universe, every minute and second brought unimaginable comprehension.

If Old Tyrant Song is me in the future, that means that one day in the future, I will dream into the state of ‘Senior Daozi proving his undying’ again, and observe the myriad practitioners in the universe through the ‘Heavenly Dao’s Vision.’

“Don’t get distracted, Shuhang,” Unknown White No. 31 said.

Even the Defiant Whale Warrior Glove on Song Shuhang’s right hand fell off.

Song Shuhang’s ‘Holy Ape Choir’ added 33 more Holy Apes to its strength!

Chapter 2984: Chapter 2982: The Delicate and Gentle Song
As the faint glow unconsciously emitted from Tyrannical Song’s right hand, the surrounding space seemed to become more amiable.

This task also needed to be noted in his memo, and marked with a star, highlighted.

Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet, Zither Master’s Claw, Black-skinned Soft Feather.

Meet Daoist Senior?

Pavilion Master Chu, are you planning to take this opportunity to enter a prolonged sleep state to slack off?

Chapter 2986: Chapter 2984: Evolution of the Sage’s Eye

but Senior White had to maintain the seal.

Chapter 2987: Chapter 2985: Comprehensive Packaging Plan
“`

“Only able to seal for twenty-two days?” Daozi rubbed his brow with a troubled expression.

Then, he looked at Tyrannical Song, who had a conflicted look on his face.

This is too hard!

Even with his support behind the scenes and Tyrannical Song’s fame that has now spread throughout the myriad practitioners in the universe... making Tyrannical Song ascend as the 9th Heavenly Dao within twenty-two days is as difficult as ascending to the heavens.

According to the historical records of previous Heavenly Dao ascensions, the battle for each one lasted at least several decades, and sometimes even several hundred years.

Sometimes, battles between Immortals of equal strength can last several years!

Thus, this short amount of time is insufficient, it’s too difficult!

“I must do something while I am still in charge,” Daozi thought to himself.

As the temporary 8.5th Heavenly Dao, he could be replaced at any time.

Unused power is wasted power.

So, while he was still the Heavenly Dao, should he give Tyrannical Song another push?

To elevate his prestige and strength to another level?

“First of all, it’s Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song’s Second Immortality Path... I must find a way for him to experience the ‘Heavenly Dao Eye’ once more, to bring him into contact with more of the ‘Heavenly Dao Immortal Knowledge’, in order to help him as much as possible to complete the Second Immortality Path. If his Second Immortality Path is perfected, his strength can definitely reach the very top tier in one fell swoop.”

Daozi had studied Song Shuhang’s Second Immortality Path and knew the complexity and power it held. It was virtually impossible to perfect without a perspective and knowledge transcending the mundane, but once perfected, it would be terrifyingly strong.

“Then... The Constant Star Destroyers and the Void Sun Guardians, I need to secretly capture a batch of them and refine them into ‘Immortality Material Elixirs’ to boost Tyrannical Song.”

After Tyrannical Song has proven his Dao for immortality, the only thing he lacks compared to veteran Immortals is the time spent in cultivation. And the ‘Immortality Material Elixir’ can help narrow the gap between Tyrannical Song and the veteran Immortals as much as possible.

“Next is prestige... Tyrannical Song’s prestige is already high in the myriad practitioners in the universe, but it can still be elevated further. For instance, we need to create headlines even more shocking than ‘slaying an undefeatable Heavenly Emperor’ like how Tyrannical Song, while still a mortal, overpowered a formidable enemy with ‘eternal attributes’ who also sought to obliterate the myriad practitioners in the universe.”

With such an accomplishment, Tyrannical Song’s prestige, coupled with the added afterward merits of being a ‘savior + slaying the eternal’, will truly reach the peak, rendering all Immortals in the myriad practitioners in the universe both respectful and convinced.

However... how to orchestrate the scene of ‘Tyrannical Song overpowering the enemy with eternal attributes’ needs further consideration.

Fortunately, the ‘Black Sun’ is already in our hands, and the antagonist can’t escape.

First, I’ll power up Tyrannical Song’s abilities then consult with ‘Fellow Daoist White’s group’ to prepare a grand event for Tyrannical Song vs. the Dark Sun.

This will also serve as a good opportunity to practice the battle experience between Tyrannical Song and the ‘Dark Sun’, so that when Tyrannical Song ascends to the Heavenly Dao in the future, he’ll be more adept at handling the ‘Dark Sun’.

Moreover, during the life and death battle against the enemy with eternal attributes, Tyrannical Song’s understanding of the ‘Second Immortality Path’ may also advance further.

After all, it’s during adversarial battles that one’s potential is truly activated!

A myriad of ideas kept surfacing in Daozi’s mind.

These ideas covered all bases, strengthening and packaging Song Shuhang from every angle without any blind spots!

After the destruction of Confucianism... in secret, Sages laid down many ‘resurrection techniques’ for their disciples. Though these resurrection techniques were somewhat incomplete, they represented hope, a channel.

Since becoming the Will of the Heavens, all Daozi needed to do was erase the imperfections of the resurrection techniques, and then allow the members of Confucianism to go through the resurrection process.

But the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion was different.

The members of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion didn’t leave behind any resurrection techniques, and too much time had passed since they were gone.

After truly hearing the news of despair, he didn’t know if Pavilion Master Chu could maintain her state of mind.

After detachment, perhaps time, space, and dimensions would all be on a different level from now.

If one truly transcended time and space, theoretically, it should be possible to extract the members of the ‘Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion’ directly from the river of time.

Chapter 2988: Chapter 2986: Do whatever you want to do!

Tyrannical Song’s desire to become the Heaven’s Will +1, Tyrannical Song’s motivation to detach from the Heaven’s Will +1.

Just like the Heaven’s Will and immortality.

Soon, he could also leave his ‘steel manifestation’ in the main world to act on his behalf.

The Three Corpses Avatar, however, needed to accompany him into the ‘time-distorted secret realm’ of Daoist Senior for cultivation.

The ‘aged White’ before him, the ‘Tribulation Crossing Avatar’ that was sliced in half, and the ‘youthful Senior White clone’ from Song Shuhang’s real illusion.

Chapter 2989: Chapter 2987: I want to sprinkle cumin on you!

Chapter 2990: Chapter 2988: Dark Song, arrange!

Chapter 2991: Chapter 2989: Qiu Youyou, Dark Song, Netherly White

She knew that Song Shuhang was aiming to prove his “eternity” as well.

One’s power is limited; to push “Tyrannical Song” to the position of the ninth Heavenly Dao, Daozi still needed the assistance of alliance members.

Among the members of the alliance, the Eight-Armed Primordial Heavenly Demon had sworn to assist Tyrannical Song in proving his Dao, Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven had a hobby of nurturing the Heavenly Dao, the Great Master of Buddha Temple held Song Shuhang, who had cultivated the ❮Basic Buddhist Fist Technique❯, in high regard, and Song Shuhang and Fairy Cheng Lin had always been Tyrannical Song’s backers.

So, when thinking about giving “Tyrannical Song” a push, Daozi immediately thought of his group of friends.

Now, with the help of the 8.5 Daozi plan, she had achieved her goal.

Above their heads.

Chapter 2994: Chapter 2992: True Transmission – Confucianism Sage Fist!
There was a deep-seated hatred between the scholarly system and the liquefied metal ball, just as there was a feud of annihilation between them and Netherworld’s fat ball.

The battle for the Heavenly Dao seat was a matter of life and death by its very nature, not child’s play. There was no option for a peaceful battle.

Hate, in many cases, doesn’t really pick sides between justice or the foulest evil.

Reality is not simply black or white.

But in any case, hate is hate.

A blood feud is a grudge.

How to repay a favor? Return the favor directly for a grudge, and repay kindness with kindness!

“I’ll just watch from the side,” the Child of the Heavenly Emperor said.

[Goudan, are you really going to do this?] As he pondered, the voice of the striped dragon suddenly rang out.

The striped dragon had clearly noticed what Cheng Lin intended to do, which was evidently to help Dark Song achieve reincarnation.

“Rest assured, Father Goudan. This time, I am quite certain that I will not shatter. Moreover, even if something unexpected happens, with you all here... you can put me back together again,” the glass-gem colored Cheng Lin said.

This time, her tone of voice had switched to another manner; now it truly sounded like Cheng Goudan’s tone and voice.

Boom~~

Across from them, Daozi’s Heavenly Dao strike descended, covering all of Fat Ball boss’s ‘liquid metal body,’ including the parts that had been dispersed by Knowledge’s Iron Fist.

After covering them, Daozi’s movements suddenly paused, stopping his action of ‘directly smashing Fat Ball to bits, so it couldn’t recondense for a hundred years.’

As a Heavenly Dao, he had an acute sense of the events about to unfold in the future.

Especially if the future events were to involve him somehow, this intuition would become even clearer.

For instance, at this moment, Daozi sensed that Cheng Lin seemed to want to perform a series of actions on ‘Dark Song,’ which appeared beneficial.

Moreover, these actions would relate to his plan of ‘pushing Tyrannical Song to become the Ninth Heavenly Dao.’

Thus, driven by intuition, Daozi stopped his action.

“Cheng Lin, what do you intend to do? Do you need my assistance?” Daozi asked Cheng Lin—his attitude towards Cheng Lin and Song Wood was one of gratitude.

“I want to use an ancient secret technique to reincarnate ‘Dark Song,’ allowing him to remain unaffected and become a fully realized Netherworld Ruler individual,” Cheng Lin explained.

At the same time, she briefly shared with others the issue about ‘the original petty ghost spirit – ghostly body’ that she had previously discussed with the Child of the Heavenly Emperor.

Heavenly Dao Father Goudan is a prodigy among the historical Heavenly Daos... Many of the things he came up with are still indecipherable to the current Heavenly Dao.

“To retain Tyrannical Song’s ‘Netherworld Ruler persona’? I see,” Daozi nodded slightly. With his current status as a Heavenly Dao, he could roughly deduce what Fairy Cheng Lin wanted to do by considering Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song’s current state.

“If you wish to preserve the ‘Netherworld Ruler’s Authority’ for the incarnation of Dark Song... then perhaps, we could go even further,” a thread of Daozi’s intent materialized and spoke out.

“The ruler of the Netherworld, huh?” Father Goudan immediately guessed Daozi’s thought.

“Yes... Anyway, if I dissipate, it will disappear once more.” Daozi’s intent looked toward the Netherworld’s Fat Ball, which he was suppressing.

He then glanced at Dark Song.

This ‘ruler of the Netherworld,’ Dark Song, actually still depended on Senior White to exist.

His Netherworld ruler privileges and power were ‘borrowed’ from Senior White and couldn’t be considered as those of a truly independent entity. He was a ‘pseudo-Netherworld ruler.’

However, Fat Ball was a genuine ‘ruler of the Netherworld,’ recognized by the Netherworld Heaven and Earth.

If Fat Ball could be used to compensate for Dark Song’s deficiencies... and if Fairy Cheng Lin could then reincarnate Dark Song, then a complete and perfect True Netherworld Ruler Tyrannical Song could be left behind.

“Is that possible?” Senior White two asked curiously.

If Qiu Youyou could be transformed into Dark Song, that would indeed be quite interesting.

At that time, Dark Song would be both Great Ruler Song and Fat Ball Ruler; incredibly powerful.

“If it were another ruler of the Netherworld, like Fellow Daoist White, for example, it would absolutely be impossible to supplement Dark Song’s deficiencies. But with Fat Ball Ruler, it’s entirely possible,” Daozi confidently stated.

Daozi briefly explained a few key points to everyone.

Firstly, Daozi had assumed the position of Heavenly Dao using the shell of the Heavenly Dao Fat Ball, suppressing Fat Ball, and knowing several of its weaknesses.

Secondly, in Daozi’s hand was an example of a successful ‘Netherworld ruler fusion’—the Black Sun, which was a special existence merged by its corresponding Heavenly Dao, using ‘immortal material.’

Daozi needed only to study the structure of the Black Sun thoroughly and, by working backward, could deduce the technique.

Coincidentally, Song Shuhang possessed an ‘undying fat whale golden core’ which should meet the requirements for fusion.

Lastly... there was the Scholarly Sage’s Eye!

After Tyrannical Song obtained a pair of Scholarly Sage’s Eyes, he had shared the related clues with Daozi.

With just the Sage’s Eye + a path to immortality, one can inherit the Sage’s ability to ‘devour existence.’

Combining these three, it suddenly seemed feasible for Tyrannical Song to use Qiu Youyou to fill the deficiencies in Dark Song.

There was no need to completely devour Qiu Youyou; just a portion needed to be devoured and fused, combined with Dark Song himself, to meet the requirements.

After concocting a complete Dark Song... then Fairy Cheng Lin could use secret techniques to reincarnate him, preserving Dark Song perfectly.

Again, Daozi, with the help of the Heavenly Dao Calculation Ability, meticulously calculated from start to finish and confirmed that the plan was feasible!

“So you mean, gnaw away part of Qiu Youyou? Not bad,” Senior White two nodded.

“I’ll give it my all, just as long as the Heavenly Emperor’s Son is willing to help me, my problem won’t be big,” Fairy Cheng Lin pondered.

“Then lastly, inheriting the innate ability of my teacher goes up on the schedule now,” Daozi said as he stretched out his hand, temporarily sealing the fat ball.

Only waiting for Song Shuhang to inherit the Sage’s ability, and once that side figured out the fusion technique for the Black Sun, this plan could commence.

“Before using the Sage’s Eyes... we should first try if we can turn the Sage’s Eyes from consumables into power banks,” Dark Song reminded.

“Brilliant, perfect,” Daozi was thrilled.

If possible, he also hoped that the eyes left by his teacher wouldn’t disappear.

“I’ll divide a portion of my spirit and lend you a helping hand on this research project. You can use my spirit to borrow Heavenly Axiom-level Calculation Ability,” Daozi promised.

Chapter 2996: Chapter 2994: Close-up Homework Schedule (Additional 1)
If he could inherit the teacher’s secret techniques without having to use up an eyeball, Daozi would be very pleased.

Although both ‘Sage’s eyes’ had already been given to Tyrannical Song, and ownership had gone over to the other party.

If it could be made recyclable, Daozi would naturally support it with all his might.

At the same time, Senior White two has a group of ‘research-oriented clones’ who will study with Cheng Lin and the ninth dragon pattern on [how to connect the Sage’s eye with the undying fat whale golden core], turning the Sage’s eye from a one-time-use battery into a power bank.

Cheng Goudan will split into two parts, with the extra part preparing to make contact with the sealed fat ball big shot in advance, getting to know the fat ball’s aura, power attributes, body data and so on in preparation for the ‘perfectly reincarnated Dark Song’.

As for the core person of this project, ‘Dark Song’, he only needs to preside over the ‘Demon Sea World’ and quietly wait for the big shots to finish their preparations.

At most, like Tyrannical Song himself, he’d occasionally act as the subject of research.

After all, the main task for Dark Song and Tyrannical Song isn’t ‘research projects,’ but closed-door cultivation.

In order to take care of Song Shuhang, and to enable researchers from both the Netherworld and the main world to conduct experiments in the same environment, Daozi thoughtfully set up Tyrannical Song’s secluded cultivation time in a rift between the Netherworld and the main world.

Thus, whether it is the ruler of Netherworld Senior White two, or Cheng Lin, Heavenly Emperor’s child, and others, they all can enter the time-distorted secret realm, and using the ‘time extension’ of the secret realm, they will be able to carve out more time for research.

Inside the time-distorted secret realm.

Song Shuhang’s main body bathed and changed clothes.

This was his first time making such formal and serious preparations for seclusion. Moreover, this time he wasn’t closing up for just a day or two, or a month or two—he was mentally prepared to be in closed-door cultivation for decades!

The connection between Song Fat Ball and the fat ball of the Netherworld Realm had now been personally shielded by Daozi—before long, once Dark Song and Qiu Youyou fully fused, Song Shuhang would become the true main body of Song Fat Ball!

At that time, the newly-born Song Qiu Youyou would become a true asset to Song Shuhang, just like Song Fat Ball is now. No longer would Tyrannical Song have to multitask and control them separately.

As for what happens after a hundred and eighty years... there’s even less worry about that.

By then, either Tyrannical Song would have proved his Dao and achieved immortality, and Song Fat Ball would forever be Song Fat Ball.

Or, everyone’s plan failed, and the myriad realms perished in the ‘Dark Sun’ scheme... if the world is doomed, what’s there to worry about?

“A study schedule? Indeed, I need such a thing,” Song Shuhang said as he threw off his cape and sat down cross-legged.

After some thought, he added two words—Plenty!

Song Shuhang’s ‘Second Immortality’ is too vast; he needs plenty of theories on the way to immortality to inspire him.

Stones from other mountains can be used to polish jade.

Any defeated foes will have to pay a price. I will bring all the losers here, and have them personally explain the mysteries of the ‘Way to Immortality’ to the main body!”

Moreover... it would be best if we had samples from the Immortals of every major race in the myriad realms. If there aren’t any Immortals for a certain power system, top Tribulation Immortals are also acceptable.”

After entering the dream of Daozi, he had gained some clues about the Second Immortality.

Different races, different power systems, whether human, monster, demon, or ghost... in the Second Immortality, they all had a place.

Moreover, the Second Immortality doesn’t need to be comprehended all at once like the First Immortality.

His Second Immortality... could be assembled modularly, piece by piece.

This possibility gave Song Shuhang hope for perfecting the Second Method.

Chapter 2997: Chapter 2995: Being Polite and Civilized (Supplement 2)
Attempting to understand the entire Second Immortality Method in one breath is overreaching, and is bound to lead to failure.

However, if one were to comprehend each small module of the path to immortality individually, and finally combine them, the seemingly impossible-to-perfect Second Method might actually become attainable.

“My path to immortality is the cycle of life and decay, related to life and death... Perhaps you can make use of it,” said Chu Pavilion Lord’s Dumb Hair. “Then, shall I start the first lesson of observing the Way to Immortality?”

What you’re about to share with me isn’t just any Daoist Canon, but the secrets of your own path to immortality. The secrets of the path to immortality are the core elements, the greatest secrets of Pavilion Master Chu’s way to immortality.

Therefore, it’s essential not to put the seniors in an embarrassing situation.

“All right, we understand these matters better than you,” said Chu Pavilion Lord’s Dumb Hair, swaying in the wind, gracefully. “If there’s anything we’re unwilling to share, there’s no need to force us. Those willing to share will explain their path to immortality without coercion.”

It’ll only be available to the seniors of the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ and a few fellow friends with whom I share a good relationship,” replied Song Shuhang. “Regarding the spirit stones earned, we’ll split them fifty-fifty.”

“That’s fine, you take care of these arrangements,” said Chu Pavilion Lord’s Dumb Hair, fluttering—she never valued spirit stones much. Back when her Crystal-clear Water Pavilion held numerous natural treasures and spirit stones, she hardly grieved over losing them.

After all, she was different from Song Shuhang; she knew how to save money!

Once her main body fully recovers, she could earn as many spirit stones as she wished.

Song Shuhang beamed with a smile.

After this episode, his ‘Cultivator Chat System’ will amass a huge collection of ‘Daoist Canon’ benefits... In the future, to view these ‘Daoist Canon’ videos, countless cultivators will renew their VIP subscriptions and spend spirit stones to watch the teachings.

A future filled with rolling riches awaited him.

And that future was not too distant... perhaps in just over a dozen days, he could become a person with spirit stones.

Since there’s a vast difference between the external world’s time and this ‘time-distorted secret realm,’ it’s imperative to hurry and bring back more treasured immortals for the main body.

For instance, those who recently lost to it on Mars could be gathered as a starting point.

By following Song as the fat ball, it could observe the status of the other party and notify Song Shuhang immediately if any issues arose with the fat ball.

Now, after being strengthened by Ruler of the Netherworld White, it had reached the level of an immortal divine weapon. Given enough spirit stones and mental energy, it could even unleash the transient power of a primordial treasure.

The fat ball’s spherical form slightly bobbed in agreement.

Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet flew and hung itself onto Song Fat Ball.

It suddenly regretted deciding to go out with Song Fat Ball.

At this moment.

The cultivators of the myriad realms were calming their hearts that had been pounding like startled deer.

In the Book World—right after the era of the Heavenly Emperor in the ancient era—a big shot who proved the path to immortality lamented.

The Book World is one of the ‘myriad realms’ special worlds, slightly smaller than the Dream Realm, and this Immortal is its ruling authority—not the Sector Lord.

His interest lies in recording significant events occurring throughout the myriad realms.

Fairy Wu Yu’s path to immortality was the special metal-based system.

Every transformation was a process of shedding the old and evolving...

Chapter 2998: Chapter 2996: When Tyrannical Song Comes Knocking
“Who?” Fairy Wu Yu reflexively responded—she felt that the voice of the fellow friend knocking from outside the Book World was very familiar, causing her hair to stand on end.

However, because the voice was deliberately kept low and sounded incredibly gentle, Fairy Wu Yu couldn’t immediately link this voice with the ‘familiar one’ from her memories.

After responding, Fairy Wu Yu turned to look at her good friend, the Immortal of the Book World.

This Book World was her friend’s territory, and even though her friend was not the official ‘Sector Lord’ of the Book World, he was the actual ruler, lacking only the official recognition.

“Whose name did I just call?” Fairy Wu Yu looked at her friend and asked.

“Tyrannical Song,” the Book World Immortal replied indifferently.

What’s going on?

I just casually mentioned Tyrannical Song, and Tyrannical Song appears knocking at the door?

How is one supposed to enjoy themselves in peace?

Moreover, I didn’t speak ill of Tyrannical Song, did I? On the contrary, I was recounting Tyrannical Song’s impressive past to my friend.

Why am I being ‘checked’ by Tyrannical Song under such circumstances?

——mainly because outside, Tyrannical Song’s voice sounded very gentle and seemed to be devoid of malice.

Polite and gentle, if we let him in, he surely wouldn’t do anything to harm me, right?

“Alright, then I will let Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song in,” the Book World Immortal said, gesturing with a hand. He added, “To be accurate, it should be a clone of Tyrannical Song. The one you saw, hammering down fellow Immortals in the universe on Mars.”

Fairy Wu Yu: “...”

“I am Fairy Wu Yu. Welcome, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song,” Fairy Wu Yu also paid respects to Tyrannical Song’s clone.

“I am Tyrannical Song’s fat ball clone, greetings to both fellow Immortals,” said Song’s fat ball, imitating the gentle tone of his main body.

This incarnation of Tyrannical Song was born for slaughter!

But en route, it suddenly heard someone calling its name.

Sensing this, it approached and knocked on the door.

This knock revealed two great surprises—two living Immortals!

Moreover, they were Immortals it had not hammered yet.

Especially this fairy, look at her body with its metal Attribute, it looked valuable at a glance and had a predestined connection with its “Liquid Metal Body”.

And the fairy’s path to immortality seemed to subtly contain an essence of “Rebirth”, vaguely related to the principles of “Life and Death”, meeting the requirements and conditions of Tyrannical Song’s main body.

The Immortal next to her, exuding a scholarly aroma, though his path to immortality was not visible, such a bookish path to immortality would surely delight Tyrannical Song’s main body as well.

The more the fat ball observed, the brighter the eyes that formed on its body became.

How wonderful!

The main body was indeed right, being polite really is a good thing.

It was precisely because it was polite that it encountered these two Immortal friends.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song’s clone, you’ve misunderstood; my good friend Fairy Wu Yu and I were just talking about your battle in place of Tyrannical Song on Mars, mentioning the name ‘Tyrannical Song’, which might have caused you passing by to sense it,” explained the Book World Immortal slightly smiling and in an organized manner.

“I see, so this is fate. [Hahaha laughter]” said the fat ball Song.

Fairy Wu Yu: “It is fate, and fate always comes in such mysterious ways.”

In short, casually chat with Tyrannical Song’s clone for a bit, then find a chance to send him away.

“Since we are fated, then Fairy Wu Yu, let’s have a battle first,” said the fat ball Song as it began to move its body around, assuming a ‘I’m going to hammer you’ posture.

Fairy Wu Yu: “!!!”

What the hell, so heartless!

Didn’t you say we had fate with you?

And your “fate” is to hammer us?

Utter madness!

Fortunately, the Book World Immortal maintained his composure: “Fellow Daoist Ball, there is no need to be hasty. Our Book World is quite small amongst the myriad practitioners in the universe, and it can’t withstand too much turmoil. Since we are fated, why don’t you first tell us what it is that you want to do? If it’s not necessary, we might be able to skip the ‘battle’ phase.”

Even with his eyes closed, the Book World Immortal continuously sensed the state of the fat ball Song.

He possessed a secret technique that allowed him to make some predictions about ‘the other party’ through things like ‘aura’.

Upon discovering himself and Fairy Wu Yu, the other party displayed an ‘excited’ aura.

Then, it seemed to ponder.

And subsequently, it suggested a battle—clearly, this clone of Tyrannical Song was searching for people like him and Fairy Wu Yu with a certain goal in mind.

He and Fairy Wu Yu shared several similarities, the most significant being their identities as Immortals.

[Now that the Will of the Heavens has proved his Dao, there is no chance to ‘compete for the Heavenly Dao seat’ in the near future; why then does Tyrannical Song still seek to provoke battles with Immortals?]

“Skip the battle?” The fat ball felt somewhat disappointed; it still wanted to do the hammering first.

At this point, Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet, who had been hanging at its waist all the while, couldn’t hold back and spoke up: “Actually, we are searching for Immortals to challenge them and hope to establish a covenant. If possible, we would like these Immortal friends to meet with Tyrannical Song’s main body.”

“Meet the main body? What for... what for?” Fairy Wu Yu was a bit panicked.

“The main body wants to understand the various Mysterious Principles of the immortal paths,” said the fat ball Song. “If you agree, Fairy, I will take you to meet my main body right now. If you disagree, then we will have a battle.”

“Don’t worry, after the fairy meets with Tyrannical Song’s main body, we will not shortchange you. The current Tyrannical Song main body is a great Treasure; just by meeting him, you are sure to gain much,” added Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet.

The fat ball Song was responsible for playing the heavy, and Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet took on the role of the good cop.

Chapter 2999: Chapter 2997: This is Tyrannical Song, How Terrifying!
Moreover, Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet did not lie—Song Shuhang, to the myriad practitioners in the universe seeking immortality, indeed represents a great treasure!

It is known that Tyrannical Song had always maintained a close connection with “Daozi.” Moreover, he had just experienced the “Heavenly Dao’s View” and exited from the dreamland.

On Song Shuhang now resided some “immortal information residues” that had been transformed by his body.

—Directly viewing immortal information, even the top Immortals would fall into eternal sleep. However, these transformed “immortal information residues” could be captured and analyzed by Immortals.

If they are lucky enough to lay down a foundation, they might be able to go further in the future and access deeper immortal information.

Not only that.

Tyrannical Song was now perfecting his “Second Path to Immortality.” During this period, he was essentially looking at things from a perspective “beyond Immortals.”

If Immortals show Tyrannical Song their “Mysterious Principles of Immortality,” they might receive some feedback from Song Shuhang, supplement themselves, and advance their path to immortality even further!

This is truly a win-win situation.

—The only difficulty is that most Immortals would not want to explain their “Mysterious Principles of Immortality” to others.

...

...

After leaving Song Shuhang, Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet exhibited its keen survival instincts!

Confronting big shots is indeed thrilling, but one can’t do such exciting things every day, right? It’s not good for the heart.

Exciting activities should be enjoyed once a month or every few months; doing them daily would be unbearable.

Thus, when fat ball was trying to steer things towards “combat,” Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet was in the background, doing his best with his verbal skills to shift things toward a “peaceful resolution.”

Any battle that can be resolved with words should avoid going to fists!

If they really cannot be resolved peacefully, then let fat ball take the stage later—it would also fully assist fat ball!

The forehead of fat ball wrinkled slightly, feeling a bit regretful for bringing along Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet.

As an avatar of the ruler of the Netherworld, it craved battle and destruction.

At its waist, the Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet, with an unprecedented strong desire to live, instantly sensed the fluctuation in fat ball’s mood and deduced its feelings.

Thus, Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet secretly transmitted a sound to fat ball: “We have limited time, the flow of time outside passes much faster than our main body in the ‘time-distorted secret realm.’ Therefore, we can’t afford to waste time, we need to try to send as many Immortal friends into the time-distorted secret realm as fast as possible, for our main body to absorb.”

“That makes sense! I almost forgot about that!” fat ball suddenly realized.

It seems that apart from the Three Corpses Avatar in its body’s pendants, which seems a bit unintelligent, the other pendants are still very reliable.

“Then, for those we can quickly resolve through verbal communication, let’s communicate well. Even if we have to resolve it through battle, I will also try to unleash the big moves right from the start, aiming to eliminate the enemies in the shortest time possible,” fat ball also secretly responded with sound transmission.

On the other side.

The corner of the mouth of the Book World Immortal twitched slightly.

Although his secret techniques could not fully decipher the detailed exchange between fat ball and Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet, through the changes in their “aura” and the transformation in fat ball’s emotions, the Book World Immortal could vaguely guess some aspects.

Such as... if they did not agree, he and his friend Fairy Wu Yu might get hammered.

“Wu Yu, if the two of us join forces... do you think we have a chance to beat the Tyrannical Song’s clone over there?” the Book World Immortal maintained a calm smile while secretly inquiring.

“If it’s only Tyrannical Song’s clone, you and I together might have a slight chance of winning. But if we include that stone tablet at his waist, I feel our chances of winning are slim,” Fairy Wu Yu responded.

She was a spectator of the Mars incident and had a very direct understanding of fat ball’s combat power.

At the same time, she noticed that the stone tablet bore four extremely frightening characters... those characters made her heart palpitate.

“Then, do you want to fight?” the Book World Immortal asked.

“Am I confused?” Fairy Wu Yu rolled her eyes.

What a silly question.

Why would I want to fight Tyrannical Song’s clone?

Even if we together could defeat Tyrannical Song’s clone, but there is still a more awesome Tyrannical Song main body behind him!

If the main body of Tyrannical Song came over and just gave a glare, we might end up getting pregnant.

As a man who ascended to the heavens with the “Will of the Heavens,” Tyrannical Song’s “Impregnating Gaze” had likely been strengthened to the level of a Confucian Sage from long ago.

In the myriad realms and heavens, there are likely not many who could withstand it.

Plus, unlike the Confucian Sages—whose characters were upright and who rarely resorted to using the “Impregnating Gaze” even in battle—

Tyrannical Song, according to reliable information, had initiated battles with the “Impregnating Gaze”!

“Then let’s not fight, and by the way, let’s go see Tyrannical Song’s main body,” said the Book World Immortal, smiling.

Honestly, he was very interested in Tyrannical Song’s main body.

Having recorded a thick volume of the “Biography of Tyrannical Song,” there was much he wanted to personally verify with Tyrannical Song.

Moreover...

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, are you searching for Immortals?” asked the Book World Immortal.

“Mister guessed exactly right,” replied Song Fat Ball politely.

“Well then, I actually hold the coordinates of several Immortals, which I could provide to Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song,” the Book World Immortal said, his eyes opening slightly, revealing a cold glint as sharp as a blade.

Song Fat Ball: “???”

He’s actually offering us the coordinates of Immortals voluntarily?

“In fact, those fellows and my Book World have a bit of a grudge. Over the centuries, there have been endless minor frictions. So, if possible, I hope Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song can pay them a visit and give them a little surprise,” said the Book World Immortal.

Fairy Wu Yu: “!!!”

So, there are such maneuvers too!

No wonder people say that scholars are the darkest.

“In a stone realm adjacent to mine, there’s a miniature fairyland called the ‘Mo Pool,’ where a ‘Ran Mo Daoist’ resides. He is a very interesting Immortal, another sovereign Immortal of the Stone Realm after the ‘Stone Emperor.’ Their lineage of Immortals has a particularly strong resilience when beaten,” the Book World Immortal recommended.

Afterward, the Book World Immortal recommended the abodes of two more Immortals to Song Fat Ball.

After making his recommendations, he began to gather his belongings and, taking Fairy Wu Yu with him, headed to the spatial gate opened by Song Fat Ball to meet the legendary Big Shot Tyrannical Song in person.

...

...

In the time-distorted secret realm.

When Fairy Wu Yu and the Book World Immortal stepped in, they immediately felt the flow of ‘time’ being twisted.

“Such a technique has completely surpassed the level of an Immortal, right?” Fairy Wu Yu was shocked right from the start.

Then, the two Immortals directed their gaze towards the location of Tyrannical Song’s main body.

There, Tyrannical Song’s dazed hair, the claws on his shoulders, and the long sword at his waist were all sparkling, radiating the brilliant light of the path to immortality.

At the same time, one Immortal after another was crossing through space to arrive.

The Great Northern Emperor, the master of the Titanium Temple, Immortal Fairy White Bones, the divine dragon of the Beast Realm, the white-robed Golden Trigram, and Sister White Dragon...

A string of ‘Immortal full moons’ was so bright it hurt to look at.

Moreover, in the vacuum, more spatial gates kept opening relentlessly.

Even more Immortal big shots were on their way!

Were Tyrannical Song’s social connections this extensive?

Or were all these beings ones Tyrannical Song had hammered before?

Either relationship illustrated the terrifying extent of Big Shot Tyrannical Song!

.

.

I’m such a salted fish, please give me a monthly pass~~~

Chapter 3000: Chapter 2998: Multithreaded Fellow Daoists Discussion
In some ways, Song Shuhang indeed had impressive connections.

Since he started his cultivation journey, the number of immortal big shots he knew and had confronted could fill more than two tables at a banquet — and even in the ancient Heavenly City at its peak, gathering the elite from myriad realms, there were only about two tables worth of immortals!

Moreover, the process of Song Shuhang inviting these immortal big shots was quite straightforward — he simply used two different messages, then mass sent them via the “Cultivator Chat System.”

One message was, “Seniors, help me out — coordinates ‘Heavenly Dao Time Secret Realm’, enter from the main world XXX coordinates or the Netherworld Realm YYY coordinates!”

This message was for the particularly close immortal big shots, such as Immortal Fairy White Bones, the Great Northern Emperor, and the White Dragon who had just witnessed Sixteen transcend her heavenly tribulation, among others...

The other message was, “Seniors, do you want immortal information? Want to touch upon the source of immortal information that only ‘immortals’ can access? Come, come to me, I will give all the immortal information to you — please enter from the main world XXX coordinates or Netherworld YYY coordinates — hurry over!”

This message was sent to some immortal big shots whom he had met, added as friends, and had a decent relationship with, like the Senior Dragon from the auxiliary book of Garre’s Holy Mountain in the Beast Realm, the recently departed white-robed Golden Trigram, and the blacksmith sovereign Great Eastern Emperor...

One message was meant to ask for help from the seniors.

The other was for the seniors to come and share treasures.

The effects of these two messages were as seen by the Book World Immortal and Fairy Wu Yu. Two groups of immortals, almost simultaneously, continuously crossed over through spatial means.

For those big shots with spatial abilities, the most convenient feature was their ability to travel!

...

...

“Happy New Year, seniors, please have a seat,” Song Shuhang said.

“Black-skinned sister, Fairy Creation, virtuous lamia, please bring some cushions over, today we shall have a good discussion with the seniors.”

“Great Northern Emperor, you’re here too? You also contacted a master from Buddha Temple? Welcome, of course welcome! No matter how many seniors come, as long as they are at the Immortal Realm, we welcome them all!”

“Senior Dragon from the Beast Realm, is everything still peaceful in the Beast Realm? You also want to call a friend? No problem, of course, no problem!”

Today, Song Shuhang, like a busy little bee, was mingling among the various big shot immortal seniors, welcoming each immortal senior as they arrived.

What’s more delightful, these invited immortal seniors usually had a few close fellow friends, and among these friends, one or two might be at the ‘Immortal’ realm as well.

Thus, just like a rolling snowball, one bringing two, and one bringing three, more and more immortals were invited.

Even if only one in ten of these invited immortals could attend, it was a win for Song Shuhang.

— After all, immortals are not common cabbages, there are only so many in the myriad realms, they truly are precious resources!

The reason Song Shuhang had such a large gathering of immortals was primarily thanks to the ancient Heavenly City.

The big shot immortals from the ancient Heavenly City era, now, many had some ties to Song Shuhang.

...

...

After hosting a round, Song Shuhang approached Book World Immortal and Fairy Wu Yu, “Happy New Year to the two fellow daoists, may I ask your esteemed titles?”

The echoes of fat ball’s presence lingered around these two, evidently, they had just been in contact with fat ball... Song Shuhang immediately understood their origins.

Now experienced in weathering great storms, Song Shuhang naturally wouldn’t point it out, but rather warmly welcomed and seated them, conversing politely and civility!

The Book World Immortal and Fairy Wu Yu exchanged glances—Tyrannical Song’s main body appeared unexpectedly kind and harmless, and when receiving people, he even gave off a refreshing aura.

Fairy Wu Yu smiled slightly and bowed, “I am Wu Yu, I have the pleasure of meeting Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, happy New Year to you.”

“I am the Book Immortal from the Book World, fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, happy New Year to you as well. I recently have been documenting some deeds regarding Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song... If you have some time, I would like to verify some of these deeds with you,” the Book World Immortal initiated.

“Documenting my deeds?” Song Shuhang was taken aback.

“Yes, the ‘Biography of Tyrannical Song,’” the Book World Immortal nodded.

“Haha, haha... If you have things you wish to verify, let’s have a good talk about them afterward,” Song Shuhang said somewhat shyly.

Hearing that someone wanted to write his biography, he felt a strange sense of embarrassment, but also thought it was very interesting and cool.

Thus, Song Shuhang took out his ‘friend QR code’ and said, “Let’s add each other as friends!”

This was an internal friend QR code, different from the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ QR code that was available to the general public. Adding this QR code meant becoming a true friend of Tyrannical Song!

After the friend operation, Song Shuhang guided the Book World Immortal and Fairy Wu Yu to their seats.

Then, he dispatched his three corpses separately to the three-eyed young senior and Senior White to pick up two former ‘spoils of war.’

These were likely still undergoing tribulation bolts and King Kun, who had turned into an egg and was collected by Senior White.

These were also two genuine Immortals, and Song Shuhang naturally wouldn’t overlook them—Immortals were treasured resources that Song Shuhang couldn’t afford to be choosy about.

Meanwhile, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword had also returned once to seek out Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven, saying he would bring a surprise back for Song Shuhang.

After the Book World Immortal sat down, he glanced around at the glaring circle of ‘Immortal full moons’ and frankly said, he had never seen so many Immortals gathered together in his lifetime!

“I’m pleased to meet all the seniors this New Year... Although I would love to catch up with the seniors, because I’m under a time constraint right now, let’s get straight to the point,” Song Shuhang seated himself cross-legged and said with a smile.

“Wait a moment, Shuhang,” Immortal Fairy White Bones raised her hand and said in a pleasant voice, “You invited so many fellow daoists in one breath, and then you want us all to share the ‘Mysterious Principles of Immortality’ together, isn’t that a bit inappropriate?”

They agreed to share the Mysterious Principles of Immortality with Song Shuhang, but that didn’t mean they were willing to share the core principles with so many other Immortals.

“Fairy, don’t worry, with help from Daozi Senior, I am well prepared,” Song Shuhang replied with a slight smile.

While speaking, a ‘law of the Heavenly Dao’ descended from the void and landed on Tyrannical Song.

Every Immortal present felt a stir in their hearts, staring at Tyrannical Song as they faintly felt a sense of enlightenment.

At that moment, Tyrannical Song made a series of fierce operations in the void.

[Ding~[Server•Cheng Goudan]Tyrannical Song has initiated a ‘Heavenly Axiom-level•One-to-One Private Tutoring Session’ with you, do you agree to start?]

The same notification popped up in the minds of all the Immortal big shots present.

All the seated Immortals exchanged glances, seeing the intention in each other’s eyes—Tyrannical Song was inviting everyone at once.

Was he planning to multi-thread, and grasp the ‘Mysterious Principles of Immortality’ of all the Immortals in one breath?

“Shuhang, is your head not going to explode?” Immortal Fairy White Bones asked.

“Don’t worry, the Heavenly Dao’s protection is with me,” Song Shuhang pointed at his head, confidently stating.
